<script>
/* ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
   SUPABASE INTEGRATION LAYER
═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════ */
const SUPA_URL = 'https://owctuymdpgzvxtyfuxkd.supabase.co';
const SUPA_KEY = 'eyJhbGciOiJIUzI1NiIsInR5cCI6IkpXVCJ9.eyJpc3MiOiJzdXBhYmFzZSIsInJlZiI6Im93Y3R1eW1kcGd6dnh0eWZ1eGtkIiwicm9sZSI6ImFub24iLCJpYXQiOjE3NzcwNzA5MjksImV4cCI6MjA5MjY0NjkyOX0.YZ_6rgVkI9QyeYwez_CVNFBqVY-JqKoV18gJ5_a91Ew';

async function supaFetch(table, method, body, params) {
  params = params || '';
  method = method || 'GET';
  const url = SUPA_URL + '/rest/v1/' + table + (params ? '?' + params : '');
  const headers = {
    'apikey': SUPA_KEY,
    'Authorization': 'Bearer ' + SUPA_KEY,
    'Content-Type': 'application/json',
  };
  if (method === 'POST') headers['Prefer'] = 'return=representation';
  if (method === 'PATCH') headers['Prefer'] = 'return=representation';
  const res = await fetch(url, { method, headers, body: body ? JSON.stringify(body) : null });
  if (!res.ok) { console.error('Supabase error:', method, table, await res.text()); return null; }
  if (res.status === 204) return true;
  return res.json();
}

async function dbSelect(table, params) { return supaFetch(table, 'GET', null, params); }
async function dbInsert(table, row) { return supaFetch(table, 'POST', row); }
async function dbUpdate(table, id, patch) {
  if (!id) { console.error('dbUpdate called with no id for table:', table); return null; }
  return supaFetch(table, 'PATCH', patch, 'id=eq.' + id);
}
async function dbDelete(table, id) { return supaFetch(table, 'DELETE', null, 'id=eq.' + id); }

async function dbUpsert(table, rows) {
  const url = SUPA_URL + '/rest/v1/' + table;
  const res = await fetch(url, {
    method: 'POST',
    headers: { 'apikey': SUPA_KEY, 'Authorization': 'Bearer ' + SUPA_KEY,
      'Content-Type': 'application/json', 'Prefer': 'resolution=merge-duplicates,return=representation' },
    body: JSON.stringify(Array.isArray(rows) ? rows : [rows])
  });
  if (!res.ok) { console.error('Upsert error:', await res.text()); return null; }
  return res.json();
}

/* ── Config ─────────────────────────────────────────────────── */
async function loadConfig() {
  const rows = await dbSelect('app_config');
  if (!rows) return;
  rows.forEach(function(r) {
    if (r.key === 'nsl_categories') nslCategories = r.value;
    if (r.key === 'ecar_categories') ecarCategories = r.value;
    if (r.key === 'suppliers') { nslSuppliers = r.value; ecarSuppliers = r.value; }
    if (r.key === 'nsl_password') nslPassword = r.value;
    if (r.key === 'ecar_password') ecarPassword = r.value;
  });
}

async function saveConfig(key, value) {
  const url = SUPA_URL + '/rest/v1/app_config?on_conflict=key';
  await fetch(url, {
    method: 'POST',
    headers: { 'apikey': SUPA_KEY, 'Authorization': 'Bearer ' + SUPA_KEY,
      'Content-Type': 'application/json', 'Prefer': 'resolution=merge-duplicates' },
    body: JSON.stringify({ key: key, value: value, updated_at: new Date().toISOString() })
  });
}

/* ── NSL data ───────────────────────────────────────────────── */
async function loadNslData() {
  const kits = await dbSelect('nsl_kit_parts', 'order=id');
  const ws = await dbSelect('nsl_ws_parts', 'order=id');
  if (kits) nslKitParts = kits.map(dbRowToNslKit);
  if (ws) nslWsParts = ws.map(dbRowToNslWs);
}

function dbRowToNslKit(r) {
  return nsl_kp(r.id, r.name, r.bin_number||'', r.category||'',
    r.req_qty||1, [r.qty_green||0,r.qty_red||0,r.qty_yellow||0,r.qty_orange||0],
    r.sr_qty_new||0, r.sr_min||1, r.supplier||'', r.supplier_part||'',
    r.unit_cost||0, r.last_order_date||'', r.last_order_price||0,
    r.sr_qty_used_good||0, r.sr_qty_used_repair||0);
}
function dbRowToNslWs(r) {
  return nsl_wp(r.id, r.name, r.bin_number||'', r.category||'',
    r.req_qty||1, [r.qty_classroom||0, r.qty_portable||0],
    r.sr_qty_new||0, r.sr_min||1, r.supplier||'', r.supplier_part||'',
    r.unit_cost||0, r.last_order_date||'', r.last_order_price||0,
    r.sr_qty_used_good||0, r.sr_qty_used_repair||0,
    r.ws_used_good||0, r.ws_used_repair||0);
}
function nslKitToDb(p) {
  return { name:p.name, bin_number:p.sku||'', category:p.cat,
    req_qty:p.reqQty, qty_green:p.qtys[0], qty_red:p.qtys[1],
    qty_yellow:p.qtys[2], qty_orange:p.qtys[3],
    sr_qty_new:p.srQty, sr_qty_used_good:p.srUsedGood||0,
    sr_qty_used_repair:p.srUsedRepair||0, sr_min:p.srMin,
    supplier:p.supplier||'', supplier_part:p.supplierPart||'',
    unit_cost:p.unitCost||0, last_order_date:p.lastOrderDate||null,
    last_order_price:p.lastOrderPrice||0 };
}
function nslWsToDb(p) {
  return { name:p.name, bin_number:p.sku||'', category:p.cat,
    req_qty:p.reqQty, qty_classroom:p.qtys[0], qty_portable:p.qtys[1],
    sr_qty_new:p.srQty, sr_qty_used_good:p.srUsedGood||0,
    sr_qty_used_repair:p.srUsedRepair||0, sr_min:p.srMin,
    ws_used_good:p.wsUsedGood||0, ws_used_repair:p.wsUsedRepair||0,
    supplier:p.supplier||'', supplier_part:p.supplierPart||'',
    unit_cost:p.unitCost||0, last_order_date:p.lastOrderDate||null,
    last_order_price:p.lastOrderPrice||0 };
}

async function persistNslKitPart(part) {
  if (!part.id) { console.warn('NSL kit part missing id, skipping persist:', part.name); return; }
  var row = nslKitToDb(part);
  var res = await dbUpdate('nsl_kit_parts', part.id, row);
  if (res) console.log('✓ Saved NSL kit:', part.name, 'id:', part.id);
  else console.error('✗ Failed to save NSL kit:', part.name, 'id:', part.id);
}
async function persistNslWsPart(part) {
  if (!part.id) { console.warn('NSL ws part missing id:', part.name); return; }
  var row = nslWsToDb(part);
  var res = await dbUpdate('nsl_ws_parts', part.id, row);
  if (res) console.log('✓ Saved NSL ws:', part.name, 'id:', part.id);
  else console.error('✗ Failed NSL ws:', part.name, 'id:', part.id);
}
async function deleteNslKitPart(id) { await dbDelete('nsl_kit_parts', id); }
async function deleteNslWsPart(id) { await dbDelete('nsl_ws_parts', id); }

/* ── E-Car data ─────────────────────────────────────────────── */
async function loadEcarData() {
  const hms = await dbSelect('ecar_hms_parts', 'order=id');
  const gob = await dbSelect('ecar_gob_parts', 'order=id');
  const ws = await dbSelect('ecar_ws_parts', 'order=id');
  if (hms) ecarHmsParts = hms.map(dbRowToEcarHms);
  if (gob) ecarGobParts = gob.map(dbRowToEcarGob);
  if (ws) ecarWsParts = ws.map(dbRowToEcarWs);
}

function dbRowToEcarHms(r) {
  return ecar_mkH(r.id, r.name, r.bin_number||'', r.category||'',

    r.sr_qty_new||0, r.sr_min||1, r.tr_qty_new||0,
    r.supplier||'', r.supplier_part||'', r.unit_cost||0,
    r.last_order_date||'', r.last_order_price||0,
    r.sr_qty_used_good||0, r.sr_qty_used_repair||0,
    r.tr_qty_used_good||0, r.tr_qty_used_repair||0);
}

    [r.qty_workstation||0,r.qty_toolbox1||0,r.qty_toolbox2||0,r.qty_toolbox3||0,r.qty_toolbox4||0],
    r.sr_qty_new||0, r.sr_min||1, r.tr_qty_new||0,

    r.last_order_date||'', r.last_order_price||0,
    r.sr_qty_used_good||0, r.sr_qty_used_repair||0,
    r.tr_qty_used_good||0, r.tr_qty_used_repair||0,
    r.ws_used_good||0, r.ws_used_repair||0);

function ecarHmsToDb(p) {
  return { name:p.name, bin_number:p.sku||'', category:p.cat, req_qty:p.reqQty,
    qty_222:p.qtys[0], qty_226:p.qtys[1], qty_227:p.qtys[2],
    qty_223:p.qtys[3], qty_224:p.qtys[4], qty_225:p.qtys[5],
    sr_qty_new:p.srQty, sr_qty_used_good:p.srUsedGood||0,
    sr_qty_used_repair:p.srUsedRepair||0, sr_min:p.srMin,
    tr_qty_new:p.trQty||0, tr_qty_used_good:p.trUsedGood||0, tr_qty_used_repair:p.trUsedRepair||0,
    supplier:p.supplier||'', supplier_part:p.supplierPart||'',
    unit_cost:p.unitCost||0, last_order_date:p.lastOrderDate||null, last_order_price:p.lastOrderPrice||0 };
}
function ecarGobToDb(p) {
  return { name:p.name, bin_number:p.sku||'', category:p.cat, req_qty:p.reqQty,
    qty_222g:p.qtys[0], qty_223g:p.qtys[1],
    sr_qty_new:p.srQty, sr_qty_used_good:p.srUsedGood||0,
    sr_qty_used_repair:p.srUsedRepair||0, sr_min:p.srMin,
    tr_qty_new:p.trQty||0, tr_qty_used_good:p.trUsedGood||0, tr_qty_used_repair:p.trUsedRepair||0,
    supplier:p.supplier||'', supplier_part:p.supplierPart||'',
    unit_cost:p.unitCost||0, last_order_date:p.lastOrderDate||null, last_order_price:p.lastOrderPrice||0 };
}
function ecarWsToDb(p) {
  return { name:p.name, bin_number:p.sku||'', category:p.cat, req_qty:p.reqQty,
    qty_workstation:p.qtys[0], qty_toolbox1:p.qtys[1], qty_toolbox2:p.qtys[2],
    qty_toolbox3:p.qtys[3], qty_toolbox4:p.qtys[4],
    sr_qty_new:p.srQty, sr_qty_used_good:p.srUsedGood||0,
    sr_qty_used_repair:p.srUsedRepair||0, sr_min:p.srMin,
    tr_qty_new:p.trQty||0, tr_qty_used_good:p.trUsedGood||0, tr_qty_used_repair:p.trUsedRepair||0,
    ws_used_good:p.wsUsedGood||0, ws_used_repair:p.wsUsedRepair||0,
    supplier:p.supplier||'', supplier_part:p.supplierPart||'',
    unit_cost:p.unitCost||0, last_order_date:p.lastOrderDate||null, last_order_price:p.lastOrderPrice||0 };
}

async function persistEcarHmsPart(part) {
  if (!part.id) { console.warn('E-Car HMS part missing id:', part.name); return; }
  var row = ecarHmsToDb(part);
  var res = await dbUpdate('ecar_hms_parts', part.id, row);
  if (res) console.log('✓ Saved HMS:', part.name, 'id:', part.id);
  else console.error('✗ Failed HMS:', part.name, 'id:', part.id);
}
async function persistEcarGobPart(part) {
  if (!part.id) { console.warn('E-Car Gob part missing id:', part.name); return; }
  var row = ecarGobToDb(part);
  var res = await dbUpdate('ecar_gob_parts', part.id, row);
  if (res) console.log('✓ Saved Gob:', part.name, 'id:', part.id);
  else console.error('✗ Failed Gob:', part.name, 'id:', part.id);
}
async function persistEcarWsPart(part) {
  if (!part.id) { console.warn('E-Car ws part missing id:', part.name); return; }
  var row = ecarWsToDb(part);
  var res = await dbUpdate('ecar_ws_parts', part.id, row);
  if (res) console.log('✓ Saved E-Car ws:', part.name, 'id:', part.id);
  else console.error('✗ Failed E-Car ws:', part.name, 'id:', part.id);
}
async function deleteEcarHmsPart(id) { await dbDelete('ecar_hms_parts', id); }
async function deleteEcarGobPart(id) { await dbDelete('ecar_gob_parts', id); }
async function deleteEcarWsPart(id) { await dbDelete('ecar_ws_parts', id); }

/* ── Trading Post DB ────────────────────────────────────────── */
async function tpLoadAll() {
  var events = await dbSelect('tp_events', 'order=created_at');
  var offers = await dbSelect('tp_offers', 'order=created_at');
  var wants = await dbSelect('tp_want_list', 'order=created_at');
  var incoming = await dbSelect('tp_incoming', 'order=created_at');
  var log = await dbSelect('tp_trade_log', 'order=created_at');
  var pending = await dbSelect('tp_pending', 'order=received_at');
  if (events) tpEvents = events.map(function(e){return e.name;});
  if (offers) tpOffers = offers.map(function(r){return {
    id:r.id, _dbId:r.id, name:r.name, sku:r.bin_number||'', prog:r.program,
    cond:r.condition, qty:r.qty, want:r.looking_for, notes:r.notes,
    event:r.event_id, status:r.status, addedDate:r.created_at};});
  if (wants) tpWantList = wants.map(function(r){return {
    id:r.id, _dbId:r.id, name:r.name, sku:r.bin_number||'',
    qty:r.qty, notes:r.notes, addedDate:r.created_at};});
  if (incoming) tpIncoming = incoming.map(function(r){return {
    id:r.id, _dbId:r.id, competitorName:r.competitor_name, team:r.team,
    event:r.event_id, date:r.created_at,
    offering:{name:r.offering_name,sku:r.offering_bin,qty:r.offering_qty,cond:r.offering_condition},
    wanting:{name:r.wanting_name,sku:r.wanting_bin,qty:r.wanting_qty},
    notes:r.notes, status:r.status};});
  if (log) tpTradeLog = log.map(function(r){return {
    id:r.id, date:r.created_at, event:r.event_id,
    competitorName:r.competitor_name, team:r.team,
    wentOut:{name:r.went_out_name,qty:r.went_out_qty,prog:r.went_out_program},
    cameIn:{name:r.came_in_name,qty:r.came_in_qty,cond:r.came_in_condition},
    notes:r.notes};});
  if (pending) tpPending = pending.map(function(r){return {
    id:r.id, _dbId:r.id, fromTradeId:r.trade_log_id,
    receivedDate:r.received_at, event:r.event_id,
    competitorName:r.competitor_name, description:r.description, qty:r.qty,
    initialCond:r.initial_condition, assessedCond:r.assessed_condition||'',
    placeTo:r.place_to||'', notes:r.notes||'', status:r.status};});
}

async function tpEnsureEvent(name, program) {
  var url = SUPA_URL + '/rest/v1/tp_events?on_conflict=name';
  var r = await fetch(url, { method:'POST',
    headers:{'apikey':SUPA_KEY,'Authorization':'Bearer '+SUPA_KEY,
      'Content-Type':'application/json','Prefer':'resolution=merge-duplicates,return=representation'},
    body: JSON.stringify({name:name, program:program}) });
  var data = await r.json();
  return data && data[0] ? data[0].id : null;
}

async function tpSaveOffer(offer) {
  var eventId = tpEvent ? await tpEnsureEvent(tpEvent, tpProgram) : null;
  var row = { name:offer.name, bin_number:offer.sku||'', program:offer.prog||tpProgram,
    condition:offer.cond, qty:offer.qty, looking_for:offer.want||'',
    notes:offer.notes||'', event_id:eventId, status:offer.status||'active' };
  if (!offer._dbId) {
    var res = await dbInsert('tp_offers', row);
    if (res && res[0]) offer._dbId = res[0].id;
  } else {
    await dbUpdate('tp_offers', offer._dbId, row);
  }
}

async function tpSaveWant(item) {
  var eventId = tpEvent ? await tpEnsureEvent(tpEvent, tpProgram) : null;
  var row = { name:item.name, bin_number:item.sku||'', qty:item.qty,
    notes:item.notes||'', event_id:eventId, source:'manual' };
  if (!item._dbId) {
    var res = await dbInsert('tp_want_list', row);
    if (res && res[0]) item._dbId = res[0].id;
  }
}

async function tpSaveIncomingRecord(record) {
  var eventId = tpEvent ? await tpEnsureEvent(tpEvent, tpProgram) : null;
  var row = { competitor_name:record.competitorName, team:record.team||'',
    event_id:eventId, offering_name:record.offering.name,
    offering_bin:record.offering.sku||'', offering_qty:record.offering.qty,
    offering_condition:record.offering.cond, wanting_name:record.wanting.name||'',
    wanting_bin:record.wanting.sku||'', wanting_qty:record.wanting.qty,
    notes:record.notes||'', status:record.status };
  var res = await dbInsert('tp_incoming', row);
  if (res && res[0]) { record._dbId = res[0].id; return res[0].id; }
  return null;
}

async function tpSaveTradeRecord(trade, incomingDbId) {
  var eventId = tpEvent ? await tpEnsureEvent(tpEvent, tpProgram) : null;
  var row = { event_id:eventId, competitor_name:trade.competitorName, team:trade.team||'',
    went_out_name:trade.wentOut.name||'', went_out_qty:trade.wentOut.qty,
    went_out_program:trade.wentOut.prog||'', came_in_name:trade.cameIn.name,
    came_in_qty:trade.cameIn.qty, came_in_condition:trade.cameIn.cond,
    notes:trade.notes||'', incoming_id:incomingDbId||null };
  var res = await dbInsert('tp_trade_log', row);
  return res && res[0] ? res[0].id : null;
}

async function tpSavePendingRecord(item, tradeLogDbId) {
  var eventId = tpEvent ? await tpEnsureEvent(tpEvent, tpProgram) : null;
  var row = { trade_log_id:tradeLogDbId||null, event_id:eventId,
    competitor_name:item.competitorName||'', description:item.description, qty:item.qty,
    initial_condition:item.initialCond||'', assessed_condition:item.assessedCond||'',
    place_to:item.placeTo||'', notes:item.notes||'', status:item.status };
  if (!item._dbId) {
    var res = await dbInsert('tp_pending', row);
    if (res && res[0]) item._dbId = res[0].id;
  } else {
    await dbUpdate('tp_pending', item._dbId, row);
  }
}

async function tpUpdateIncomingStatus(record) {
  if (record._dbId) await dbUpdate('tp_incoming', record._dbId, {status:record.status});
}

async function tpUpdatePendingStatus(item) {
  if (item._dbId) await dbUpdate('tp_pending', item._dbId, {
    assessed_condition:item.assessedCond||'', place_to:item.placeTo||'',
    notes:item.notes||'', status:item.status,
    resolved_at:new Date().toISOString() });
}

async function tpDeleteOffer(offer) { if (offer._dbId) await dbDelete('tp_offers', offer._dbId); }
async function tpDeleteWant(item) { if (item._dbId) await dbDelete('tp_want_list', item._dbId); }

/* ── Loading overlay ────────────────────────────────────────── */
function showLoadingOverlay() {
  var div = document.createElement('div');
  div.id = 'db-loading';
  div.innerHTML = '<div style="position:fixed;inset:0;background:rgba(255,255,255,0.95);z-index:9999;display:flex;flex-direction:column;align-items:center;justify-content:center;gap:16px;"><div style="width:48px;height:48px;border:4px solid #e5e5e3;border-top-color:#185FA5;border-radius:50%;animation:dbspin 0.8s linear infinite;"></div><div style="font-size:14px;font-weight:500;color:#185FA5;">Loading inventory...</div><div style="font-size:12px;color:#888;">Connecting to database</div></div><style>@keyframes dbspin{to{transform:rotate(360deg)}}</style>';
  document.body.appendChild(div);
}
function hideLoadingOverlay() {
  var el = document.getElementById('db-loading');
  if (el) el.remove();
}


/* ── SUPABASE KEEPALIVE ─────────────────────────────────────── */
async function keepAlive() {
  try {
    await supaFetch('app_config', 'GET', null, 'key=eq.suppliers&select=key');
    console.log('Supabase ping OK — ' + new Date().toLocaleTimeString());
  } catch(e) {
    console.warn('Keepalive ping failed:', e);
  }
}
// Ping every 10 minutes
setInterval(keepAlive, 10 * 60 * 1000);

/* ── Master startup load ────────────────────────────────────── */
async function loadAllData() {
  showLoadingOverlay();
  try {
    await loadConfig();
    await loadNslData();
    await loadEcarData();
    await tpLoadAll();
  } catch(e) {
    console.error('DB load error:', e);
  } finally {
    hideLoadingOverlay();
    updateHomePills();
  }
}

/* ── SHELL ────────────────────────────────────────────────── */

/* ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
   HOME SCREEN & MODULE NAVIGATION
═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════ */
let activeModule = null;

function showHome(){
  document.getElementById('home-screen').style.display='block';
  document.getElementById('nsl-module').classList.remove('active');
  document.getElementById('ecar-module').classList.remove('active');
  document.getElementById('tp-module').classList.remove('active');
  document.getElementById('dashboard-module').classList.remove('active');
  activeModule=null;
  updateHomePills();
}

function showModule(mod){
  document.getElementById('home-screen').style.display='none';
  document.getElementById('nsl-module').classList.remove('active');
  document.getElementById('ecar-module').classList.remove('active');
  document.getElementById('tp-module').classList.remove('active');
  document.getElementById('dashboard-module').classList.remove('active');
  activeModule=mod;
  if(mod==='nsl'){
    document.getElementById('nsl-module').classList.add('active');
    nsl_populateCatDropdowns();nsl_populateSupDropdowns();nsl_renderKits();
  } else if(mod==='ecar'){
    document.getElementById('ecar-module').classList.add('active');
    ecar_populateCatDropdowns();ecar_populateSupDropdowns();ecar_renderCars();
  } else if(mod==='trading'){
    showTradingPost();
  } else if(mod==='dashboard'){
    document.getElementById('dashboard-module').classList.add('active');
  }
}

function updateHomePills(){
  // NSL status
  try {
    const nslLow=nslKitParts.filter(i=>i.qtys.some((q,ki)=>q<i.reqQty)&&i.qtys.some((q,ki)=>q>0)).length;
    const nslOut=nslKitParts.filter(i=>i.qtys.some(q=>q===0)).length;
    const srLow=[...nslKitParts,...nslWsParts].filter(i=>i.srQty<=i.srMin).length;
    let nslPills='';
    if(nslOut>0) nslPills+=`<span class="status-pill pill-red">${nslOut} kit out</span>`;
    if(nslLow>0) nslPills+=`<span class="status-pill pill-amber">${nslLow} kit low</span>`;
    if(srLow>0) nslPills+=`<span class="status-pill pill-amber">${srLow} SR low</span>`;
    if(!nslPills) nslPills='<span class="status-pill pill-green">All stocked</span>';
    document.getElementById('nsl-status-pills').innerHTML=nslPills;
  } catch(e){}

  // E-Car status
  try {
    const ecarKitOut=[...ecarHmsParts,...ecarGobParts].filter(i=>i.qtys.some(q=>q===0)).length;
    const ecarKitLow=[...ecarHmsParts,...ecarGobParts].filter(i=>i.qtys.some((q,ki)=>q<i.reqQty&&q>0)).length;
    const ecarSrLow=[...ecarHmsParts,...ecarGobParts,...ecarWsParts].filter(i=>i.srQty<=i.srMin).length;
    let ecarPills='';
    if(ecarKitOut>0) ecarPills+=`<span class="status-pill pill-red">${ecarKitOut} pit out</span>`;
    if(ecarKitLow>0) ecarPills+=`<span class="status-pill pill-amber">${ecarKitLow} pit low</span>`;
    if(ecarSrLow>0) ecarPills+=`<span class="status-pill pill-amber">${ecarSrLow} SR low</span>`;
    if(!ecarPills) ecarPills='<span class="status-pill pill-green">All stocked</span>';
    document.getElementById('ecar-status-pills').innerHTML=ecarPills;
  } catch(e){}

  // Trading post pending
  try {
    const pending=tpPending.filter(p=>p.status==='pending').length;
    const el=document.getElementById('tp-home-status');
    if(el){
      if(pending>0){
        el.textContent=`${pending} item${pending>1?'s':''} pending intake`;
        el.className='status-pill pill-amber';
      } else {
        el.textContent='Ready';
        el.className='status-pill pill-green';
      }
    }
  } catch(e){}
}

document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', function(){
  const nslPwd=document.getElementById('nsl-pwd-input');
  if(nslPwd) nslPwd.addEventListener('keydown',e=>{if(e.key==='Enter')nsl_checkPwd();});
  const ecarPwd=document.getElementById('ecar-pwd-input');
  if(ecarPwd) ecarPwd.addEventListener('keydown',e=>{if(e.key==='Enter')ecar_checkPwd();});
  // Load all data from Supabase on startup
  loadAllData();
});

/*
  KIT PART: {id,name,sku,cat,reqQty,qtys:[g,r,y,o],srQty(new),srUsedGood,srUsedRepair,srMin}
  WS PART:  {id,name,sku,cat,reqQty,qtys:[classroom,portable],srQty(new),srUsedGood,srUsedRepair,srMin,wsUsedGood,wsUsedRepair}

  srQty      — stock room NEW quantity (drives reorder logic)
  srUsedGood — stock room used-serviceable quantity
  srUsedRepair — stock room used-needs-repair (tracked, not deployable)
  wsUsedGood / wsUsedRepair — same split for workspace locations
  Kits are new-only — no used tracking.
  Shared SKUs sync srQty across catalogs.
*/

function nsl_toast(msg,dur=2800){const el=document.getElementById('nsl-toast');el.textContent=msg;el.classList.add('show');setTimeout(()=>el.classList.remove('show'),dur);}
function nsl_esc(s){return(s||'').replace(/&/g,'&amp;').replace(/"/g,'&quot;').replace(/</g,'&lt;');}

function nsl_kitQtyStatus(item,ki){
  const q=item.qtys[ki];
  if(q===0) return'out';
  if(q<item.reqQty) return'low';
  return'ok';
}
function nsl_wsQtyStatus(item,wi){
  const q=item.qtys[wi];
  if(q===0) return'out';
  if(q<item.reqQty) return'low';
  return'ok';
}
function nsl_srStatus(srQty,srMin){
  if(srQty===0) return'out';
  if(srQty<=srMin) return'low';
  return'ok';
}
function nsl_worstStatus(statuses){
  if(statuses.includes('out')) return'out';
  if(statuses.includes('low')) return'low';
  return'ok';
}
function nsl_badge(s){
  if(s==='ok') return'<span class="badge bs">OK</span>';
  if(s==='low') return'<span class="badge bw">Low</span>';
  return'<span class="badge bd">Out</span>';
}

function nsl_populateCatDropdowns(){
  const opts=nslCategories.map(c=>`<option value="${nsl_esc(c)}">${nsl_esc(c)}</option>`).join('');
  const filterOpts='<option value="">All categories</option>'+opts;
  ['nsl-kits-fcat','nsl-ws-fcat','nsl-sr-fcat','nsl-master-fcat',
   'nsl-kf-cat','nsl-wf-cat','nsl-kp-fcat','nsl-wp-fcat'].forEach(id=>{
    const el=document.getElementById(id);if(!el)return;
    const prev=el.value;
    const isFilter=['nsl-kits-fcat','nsl-ws-fcat','nsl-sr-fcat','nsl-master-fcat','nsl-kp-fcat','nsl-wp-fcat'].includes(id);
    el.innerHTML=isFilter?filterOpts:opts;
    if(prev)el.value=prev;
  });
}

/* ═══════════════════════════════════
   STOCK ROOM — merged view of all items
   Each unique SKU has one srQty & srMin
   (whichever catalog defines it first wins;
    shared SKUs show combined demand)
════════════════════════════════════ */
function nsl_buildSrItems(){
  /* Merge kit parts and ws parts by SKU for SR view */
  const map=new Map();
  [...nslKitParts,...nslWsParts].forEach(item=>{
    if(!map.has(item.sku)){
      map.set(item.sku,{
        name:item.name, sku:item.sku, cat:item.cat,
        srQty:item.srQty, srMin:item.srMin,
        sourceIds:[{type:item.qtys.length===4?'kit':'ws',id:item.id}]
      });
    } else {
      const ex=map.get(item.sku);
      ex.sourceIds.push({type:item.qtys.length===4?'kit':'ws',id:item.id});
      /* Use highest srMin across all users of this SKU */
      ex.srMin=Math.max(ex.srMin,item.srMin);
      /* srQty is shared — only store once (already set) */
    }
  });
  return Array.from(map.values());
}

function nsl_getSrQtyForSku(sku){
  const nsl_kp=nslKitParts.find(i=>i.sku===sku);
  if(kp) return{srQty:kp.srQty,srMin:kp.srMin};
  const nsl_wp=nslWsParts.find(i=>i.sku===sku);
  if(wp) return{srQty:wp.srQty,srMin:wp.srMin};
  return{srQty:0,srMin:0};
}

function nsl_setSrQtyForSku(sku,newQty){
  nslKitParts.filter(i=>i.sku===sku).forEach(i=>i.srQty=newQty);
  nslWsParts.filter(i=>i.sku===sku).forEach(i=>i.srQty=newQty);
}
function nsl_setSrMinForSku(sku,newMin){
  nslKitParts.filter(i=>i.sku===sku).forEach(i=>i.srMin=newMin);
  nslWsParts.filter(i=>i.sku===sku).forEach(i=>i.srMin=newMin);
}

/* ═══════════════════════════════════
   PAGE NAV
════════════════════════════════════ */
function nsl_gotoPage(p){
  document.querySelectorAll('#nsl-module .page').forEach(x=>x.classList.remove('active'));
  document.querySelectorAll('#nsl-module .nav-tab').forEach(x=>x.classList.remove('active'));
  document.getElementById('nsl-page-'+p).classList.add('active');
  document.getElementById('nsl-nav-'+p).classList.add('active');
  nslActivePage=p;
  if(p==='kits') nsl_renderKits();
  else if(p==='workstations') nsl_renderWorkstations();
  else if(p==='stockroom') nsl_renderStockRoom();
  else if(p==='master') nsl_renderMaster();
  else if(p==='setup') nsl_renderSetup();
}

/* ═══════════════════════════════════
   nslPassword / SETUP LOCK
════════════════════════════════════ */
function nsl_clickSetup(){
  if(nslSetupUnlocked){nsl_gotoPage('setup');return;}
  document.getElementById('nsl-pwd-input').value='';
  document.getElementById('nsl-pwd-err').textContent='';
  document.getElementById('nsl-pwd-overlay').classList.add('open');
  setTimeout(()=>document.getElementById('nsl-pwd-input').focus(),80);
}
function nsl_closePwd(){document.getElementById('nsl-pwd-overlay').classList.remove('open');}
function nsl_checkPwd(){
  const v=document.getElementById('nsl-pwd-input').value;
  if(v===nslPassword){
    nsl_closePwd();nslSetupUnlocked=true;
    document.getElementById('nsl-setup-locked-bar').style.display='none';
    document.getElementById('nsl-setup-content').style.display='block';
    document.getElementById('nsl-setup-tab-label').textContent='Setup ✓';
    nsl_gotoPage('setup');
  } else {
    const f=document.getElementById('nsl-pwd-input');
    f.classList.add('shake');
    document.getElementById('nsl-pwd-err').textContent='Incorrect password.';
    f.value='';
    setTimeout(()=>f.classList.remove('shake'),350);
  }
}
function nsl_lockSetup(){
  nslSetupUnlocked=false;
  document.getElementById('nsl-setup-locked-bar').style.display='flex';
  document.getElementById('nsl-setup-content').style.display='none';
  document.getElementById('nsl-setup-tab-label').textContent='Setup';
  nsl_gotoPage('kits');nsl_toast('Setup locked');
}
function nsl_changePassword(){
  const p1=document.getElementById('nsl-np1').value.trim();
  const p2=document.getElementById('nsl-np2').value.trim();
  const msg=document.getElementById('nsl-pwd-msg');
  if(!p1){msg.style.color='#dc3545';msg.textContent='Cannot be empty.';return;}
  if(p1!==p2){msg.style.color='#dc3545';msg.textContent='Passwords do not match.';return;}
  if(p1.length<3){msg.style.color='#dc3545';msg.textContent='Minimum 3 characters.';return;}
  nslPassword=p1;
  document.getElementById('nsl-np1').value='';document.getElementById('nsl-np2').value='';
  msg.style.color='#2E7D32';msg.textContent='Password updated ✓';
  setTimeout(()=>msg.textContent='',3000);nsl_toast('Password changed ✓');
}

/* ═══════════════════════════════════
   CATEGORIES
════════════════════════════════════ */
const NSL_DEFAULT_CATS=['Drivetrain','Suspension','Body & Chassis','Electronics','Tires & Wheels','Fasteners','Consumables'];
function nsl_renderCatList(){
  document.getElementById('nsl-cat-list').innerHTML=nslCategories.map(c=>`
    <span class="cat-pill">${nsl_esc(c)}${!NSL_DEFAULT_CATS.includes(c)?`<span class="cat-del" onclick="nsl_deleteCategory('${nsl_esc(c)}')" title="Remove">×</span>`:''}</span>`).join('');
}
function nsl_addCategory(){
  const inp=document.getElementById('nsl-new-cat');
  const name=inp.value.trim();
  if(!name)return;
  if(nslCategories.includes(name)){nsl_toast('Category already exists');return;}
  nslCategories.push(name);inp.value='';
  nsl_renderCatList();nsl_populateCatDropdowns();saveConfig('nsl_categories',nslCategories);nsl_toast(`"${name}" added`);
}
function nsl_deleteCategory(name){
  if([...nslKitParts,...nslWsParts].some(i=>i.cat===name)){nsl_toast(`"${name}" is in use — reassign parts first`,4000);return;}
  if(!confirm(`Remove category "${name}"?`))return;
  nslCategories=nslCategories.filter(c=>c!==name);
  nsl_renderCatList();nsl_populateCatDropdowns();nsl_toast(`"${name}" removed`);
}

/* ═══════════════════════════════════
   SETUP RENDER
════════════════════════════════════ */

/* ── SUPPLIERS ── */
function nsl_renderSupList(){
  document.getElementById('nsl-sup-list').innerHTML=nslSuppliers.sort().map(s=>
    `<span class="sup-pill">${nsl_esc(s)}<span class="sup-del" onclick="nsl_deleteSup('${nsl_esc(s)}')" title="Remove">×</span></span>`
  ).join('');
}
function nsl_addSupplier(){
  const inp=document.getElementById('nsl-new-sup');
  const name=inp.value.trim();
  if(!name)return;
  if(nslSuppliers.includes(name)){nsl_toast('Supplier already exists');return;}
  nslSuppliers.push(name);nslSuppliers.sort();inp.value='';
  nsl_renderSupList();nsl_populateSupDropdowns();nsl_toast('\"'+name+'\" added');
}
function nsl_deleteSup(name){
  const inUse=[...nslKitParts,...nslWsParts].some(i=>i.supplier===name);
  if(inUse){nsl_toast('\"'+name+'\" is used by existing parts — reassign first',4000);return;}
  if(!confirm('Remove supplier \"'+name+'\"?'))return;
  nslSuppliers=nslSuppliers.filter(s=>s!==name);
  nsl_renderSupList();nsl_populateSupDropdowns();
}
function nsl_populateSupDropdowns(){
  const opts='<option value="">— Select supplier —</option>'+nslSuppliers.sort().map(s=>`<option value="${nsl_esc(s)}">${nsl_esc(s)}</option>`).join('');
  document.querySelectorAll('#nsl-module .sup-select').forEach(el=>{
    const prev=el.value;
    el.innerHTML=opts;
    if(prev)el.value=prev;
  });
}

function nsl_renderSetup(){
  nsl_renderCatList();nsl_renderSupList();nsl_populateCatDropdowns();nsl_populateSupDropdowns();
  nsl_renderKpList();
  nsl_renderWpList();
}

function nsl_renderKpList(){
  const s=(document.getElementById('nsl-kp-srch').value||'').toLowerCase();
  const fc=document.getElementById('nsl-kp-fcat').value||'';
  const items=nslKitParts.filter(i=>{
    if(s&&!i.name.toLowerCase().includes(s)&&!i.sku.toLowerCase().includes(s))return false;
    if(fc&&i.cat!==fc)return false;
    return true;
  });
  document.getElementById('nsl-kit-parts-count').textContent=`${items.length} of ${nslKitParts.length}`;
  const tb=document.getElementById('nsl-kp-tbody');
  if(!items.length){tb.innerHTML='<tr><td colspan="9" style="text-align:center;padding:1.5rem;color:#888">No parts found</td></tr>';return;}
  tb.innerHTML=items.map(item=>{
    const totalInKits=item.qtys.reduce((a,b)=>a+b,0);
    return`<tr>
      <td><input class="inline-input" value="${nsl_esc(item.name)}" style="width:100%;" onchange="nsl_kpSetField(${item.id},'name',this.value)"/></td>
      <td><input class="inline-input" value="${nsl_esc(item.sku)}" style="width:100%;font-family:monospace;font-size:11px;" onchange="nsl_kpSetField(${item.id},'sku',this.value)"/></td>
      <td><select class="inline-input" style="width:100%;padding:3px 4px;" onchange="nsl_kpSetField(${item.id},'cat',this.value)">
        ${nslCategories.map(c=>`<option${c===item.cat?' selected':''}>${nsl_esc(c)}</option>`).join('')}
      </select></td>
      <td><input class="inline-input" type="number" min="0" value="${item.reqQty}" style="width:48px;" onchange="nsl_kpSetField(${item.id},'reqQty',this.value)"/></td>
      <td>
        <div style="display:flex;align-items:center;gap:4px;">
          <input class="inline-input" type="number" min="0" id="rk-${item.id}" placeholder="qty" style="width:44px;"/>
          <button class="btn btn-sm" onclick="nsl_resetKitQty(${item.id})" style="white-space:nowrap;font-size:10px;">Apply all</button>
        </div>
      </td>
      <td><input class="inline-input" type="number" min="0" value="${item.srQty}" style="width:52px;" onchange="nsl_kpSetField(${item.id},'srQty',this.value)"/></td>
      <td><input class="inline-input" type="number" min="0" value="${item.srMin}" style="width:52px;" onchange="nsl_kpSetField(${item.id},'srMin',this.value)"/></td>
      <td style="text-align:center;color:#666;font-size:12px;">${totalInKits}</td>
      <td><button class="del-btn" onclick="nsl_deleteKitPart(${item.id})">Remove</button></td>
    </tr>`;
  }).join('');
}

function nsl_renderWpList(){
  const s=(document.getElementById('nsl-wp-srch').value||'').toLowerCase();
  const fc=document.getElementById('nsl-wp-fcat').value||'';
  const items=nslWsParts.filter(i=>{
    if(s&&!i.name.toLowerCase().includes(s)&&!i.sku.toLowerCase().includes(s))return false;
    if(fc&&i.cat!==fc)return false;
    return true;
  });
  document.getElementById('nsl-ws-parts-count').textContent=`${items.length} of ${nslWsParts.length}`;
  const tb=document.getElementById('nsl-wp-tbody');
  if(!items.length){tb.innerHTML='<tr><td colspan="9" style="text-align:center;padding:1.5rem;color:#888">No items found</td></tr>';return;}
  tb.innerHTML=items.map(item=>{
    const totalInWs=item.qtys.reduce((a,b)=>a+b,0);
    return`<tr>
      <td><input class="inline-input" value="${nsl_esc(item.name)}" style="width:100%;" onchange="nsl_wpSetField(${item.id},'name',this.value)"/></td>
      <td><input class="inline-input" value="${nsl_esc(item.sku)}" style="width:100%;font-family:monospace;font-size:11px;" onchange="nsl_wpSetField(${item.id},'sku',this.value)"/></td>
      <td><select class="inline-input" style="width:100%;padding:3px 4px;" onchange="nsl_wpSetField(${item.id},'cat',this.value)">
        ${nslCategories.map(c=>`<option${c===item.cat?' selected':''}>${nsl_esc(c)}</option>`).join('')}
      </select></td>
      <td><input class="inline-input" type="number" min="0" value="${item.reqQty}" style="width:48px;" onchange="nsl_wpSetField(${item.id},'reqQty',this.value)"/></td>
      <td>
        <div style="display:flex;align-items:center;gap:4px;">
          <input class="inline-input" type="number" min="0" id="rw-${item.id}" placeholder="qty" style="width:44px;"/>
          <button class="btn btn-sm" onclick="nsl_resetWsQty(${item.id})" style="white-space:nowrap;font-size:10px;">Apply both</button>
        </div>
      </td>
      <td><input class="inline-input" type="number" min="0" value="${item.srQty}" style="width:52px;" onchange="nsl_wpSetField(${item.id},'srQty',this.value)"/></td>
      <td><input class="inline-input" type="number" min="0" value="${item.srMin}" style="width:52px;" onchange="nsl_wpSetField(${item.id},'srMin',this.value)"/></td>
      <td style="text-align:center;color:#666;font-size:12px;">${totalInWs}</td>
      <td><button class="del-btn" onclick="nsl_deleteWsPart(${item.id})">Remove</button></td>
    </tr>`;
  }).join('');
}

function nsl_kpSetField(id,f,v){
  const it=nslKitParts.find(x=>x.id===id);if(!it)return;
  // persist after field update (at bottom of function)
  if(f==='name')it.name=v.trim()||it.name;
  else if(f==='sku')it.sku=v.trim();
  else if(f==='cat')it.cat=v;
  else if(f==='reqQty')it.reqQty=Math.max(0,parseInt(v)||0);
  else if(f==='srQty'){it.srQty=Math.max(0,parseInt(v)||0);nsl_syncSrQtyBySku(it.sku,it.srQty);}
  else if(f==='srUsedGood'){it.srUsedGood=Math.max(0,parseInt(v)||0);nsl_syncSrUsedGoodBySku(it.sku,it.srUsedGood);}
  else if(f==='srUsedRepair'){it.srUsedRepair=Math.max(0,parseInt(v)||0);nsl_syncSrUsedRepairBySku(it.sku,it.srUsedRepair);}
  else if(f==='srMin'){it.srMin=Math.max(0,parseInt(v)||0);nsl_syncSrMinBySku(it.sku,it.srMin);}
  else if(f==='supplier')it.supplier=v;
  else if(f==='supplierPart')it.supplierPart=v.trim();
  else if(f==='unitCost')it.unitCost=Math.max(0,parseFloat(v)||0);
  else if(f==='lastOrderDate')it.lastOrderDate=v;
  else if(f==='lastOrderPrice')it.lastOrderPrice=Math.max(0,parseFloat(v)||0);
  nsl_renderAllViews();
}
function nsl_wpSetField(id,f,v){
  const it=nslWsParts.find(x=>x.id===id);if(!it)return;
  if(f==='name')it.name=v.trim()||it.name;
  else if(f==='sku')it.sku=v.trim();
  else if(f==='cat')it.cat=v;
  else if(f==='reqQty')it.reqQty=Math.max(0,parseInt(v)||0);
  else if(f==='srQty'){it.srQty=Math.max(0,parseInt(v)||0);nsl_syncSrQtyBySku(it.sku,it.srQty);}
  else if(f==='srUsedGood'){it.srUsedGood=Math.max(0,parseInt(v)||0);nsl_syncSrUsedGoodBySku(it.sku,it.srUsedGood);}
  else if(f==='srUsedRepair'){it.srUsedRepair=Math.max(0,parseInt(v)||0);nsl_syncSrUsedRepairBySku(it.sku,it.srUsedRepair);}
  else if(f==='wsUsedGood')it.wsUsedGood=Math.max(0,parseInt(v)||0);
  else if(f==='wsUsedRepair')it.wsUsedRepair=Math.max(0,parseInt(v)||0);
  else if(f==='srMin'){it.srMin=Math.max(0,parseInt(v)||0);nsl_syncSrMinBySku(it.sku,it.srMin);}
  else if(f==='supplier')it.supplier=v;
  else if(f==='supplierPart')it.supplierPart=v.trim();
  else if(f==='unitCost')it.unitCost=Math.max(0,parseFloat(v)||0);
  else if(f==='lastOrderDate')it.lastOrderDate=v;
  else if(f==='lastOrderPrice')it.lastOrderPrice=Math.max(0,parseFloat(v)||0);
  nsl_renderAllViews();
  persistNslWsPart(it);
}
/* Sync shared SKU quantities across both catalogs */
function nsl_syncSrQtyBySku(sku,qty){
  nslKitParts.filter(i=>i.sku===sku).forEach(i=>i.srQty=qty);
  nslWsParts.filter(i=>i.sku===sku).forEach(i=>i.srQty=qty);
}
function nsl_syncSrUsedGoodBySku(sku,qty){
  nslKitParts.filter(i=>i.sku===sku).forEach(i=>i.srUsedGood=qty);
  nslWsParts.filter(i=>i.sku===sku).forEach(i=>i.srUsedGood=qty);
}
function nsl_syncSrUsedRepairBySku(sku,qty){
  nslKitParts.filter(i=>i.sku===sku).forEach(i=>i.srUsedRepair=qty);
  nslWsParts.filter(i=>i.sku===sku).forEach(i=>i.srUsedRepair=qty);
}
function nsl_syncSrMinBySku(sku,min){
  nslKitParts.filter(i=>i.sku===sku).forEach(i=>i.srMin=min);
  nslWsParts.filter(i=>i.sku===sku).forEach(i=>i.srMin=min);
}

function nsl_resetKitQty(id){
  const it=nslKitParts.find(x=>x.id===id);if(!it)return;
  const inp=document.getElementById('rk-'+id);
  const v=parseInt(inp?.value);
  if(isNaN(v)||v<0){nsl_toast('Enter a valid quantity');return;}
  it.qtys=[v,v,v,v];inp.value='';
  nsl_renderAllViews();nsl_renderKpList();
  nsl_toast(`All 4 kits set to ${v} for "${it.name}"`);
}
function nsl_resetWsQty(id){
  const it=nslWsParts.find(x=>x.id===id);if(!it)return;
  const inp=document.getElementById('rw-'+id);
  const v=parseInt(inp?.value);
  if(isNaN(v)||v<0){nsl_toast('Enter a valid quantity');return;}
  it.qtys=[v,v];inp.value='';
  nsl_renderAllViews();nsl_renderWpList();
  nsl_toast(`Both workstations set to ${v} for "${it.name}"`);
}

function nsl_addKitPart(){
  const name=document.getElementById('nsl-kf-name').value.trim();
  if(!name){nsl_toast('Enter a part name');return;}
  const kqty=parseInt(document.getElementById('nsl-kf-kqty').value)||0;
  nslKitParts.push({
    id:nslNextKitId++,name,
    sku:document.getElementById('nsl-kf-sku').value.trim(),
    cat:document.getElementById('nsl-kf-cat').value,
    reqQty:parseInt(document.getElementById('nsl-kf-req').value)||1,
    qtys:[kqty,kqty,kqty,kqty],
    srQty:parseInt(document.getElementById('nsl-kf-srqty').value)||0,
    srMin:parseInt(document.getElementById('nsl-kf-srmin').value)||1,
    supplier:document.getElementById('nsl-kf-sup').value,
    supplierPart:document.getElementById('nsl-kf-suppart').value.trim(),
    unitCost:parseFloat(document.getElementById('nsl-kf-cost').value)||0,
    lastOrderDate:'',lastOrderPrice:0,
  });
  ['kf-name','kf-sku'].forEach(id=>document.getElementById(id).value='');
  document.getElementById('nsl-kf-req').value=1;
  document.getElementById('nsl-kf-kqty').value=0;
  document.getElementById('nsl-kf-srqty').value=0;
  document.getElementById('nsl-kf-srmin').value=1;
  nsl_renderSetup();nsl_renderAllViews();nsl_toast(`"${name}" added to kit catalog`);
}
function nsl_addWsPart(){
  const name=document.getElementById('nsl-wf-name').value.trim();
  if(!name){nsl_toast('Enter an item name');return;}
  const wqty=parseInt(document.getElementById('nsl-wf-wqty').value)||0;
  nslWsParts.push({
    id:nslNextWsId++,name,
    sku:document.getElementById('nsl-wf-sku').value.trim(),
    cat:document.getElementById('nsl-wf-cat').value,
    reqQty:parseInt(document.getElementById('nsl-wf-req').value)||1,
    qtys:[wqty,wqty],
    srQty:parseInt(document.getElementById('nsl-wf-srqty').value)||0,
    srMin:parseInt(document.getElementById('nsl-wf-srmin').value)||1,
    supplier:document.getElementById('nsl-wf-sup').value,
    supplierPart:document.getElementById('nsl-wf-suppart').value.trim(),
    unitCost:parseFloat(document.getElementById('nsl-wf-cost').value)||0,
    lastOrderDate:'',lastOrderPrice:0,
  });
  ['wf-name','wf-sku'].forEach(id=>document.getElementById(id).value='');
  document.getElementById('nsl-wf-req').value=1;
  document.getElementById('nsl-wf-wqty').value=0;
  document.getElementById('nsl-wf-srqty').value=0;
  document.getElementById('nsl-wf-srmin').value=1;
  nsl_renderSetup();nsl_renderAllViews();nsl_toast(`"${name}" added to workstation catalog`);
}
function nsl_deleteKitPart(id){
  const it=nslKitParts.find(x=>x.id===id);if(!it)return;
  if(!confirm(`Remove "${it.name}" from kit catalog?\n\nThis cannot be undone.`))return;
  deleteNslKitPart(id);
  nslKitParts=nslKitParts.filter(x=>x.id!==id);
  nsl_renderSetup();nsl_renderAllViews();nsl_toast(`"${it.name}" removed`);
}
function nsl_deleteWsPart(id){
  const it=nslWsParts.find(x=>x.id===id);if(!it)return;
  if(!confirm(`Remove "${it.name}" from workstation catalog?\n\nThis cannot be undone.`))return;
  deleteNslWsPart(id);
  nslWsParts=nslWsParts.filter(x=>x.id!==id);
  nsl_renderSetup();nsl_renderAllViews();nsl_toast(`"${it.name}" removed`);
}

/* ═══════════════════════════════════
   KITS PAGE
════════════════════════════════════ */
function nsl_renderKits(){
  const s=document.getElementById('nsl-kits-srch').value.toLowerCase();
  const fc=document.getElementById('nsl-kits-fcat').value;
  const fs=document.getElementById('nsl-kits-fstk').value;
  const hint=document.getElementById('nsl-kits-hint');
  const thead=document.getElementById('nsl-kits-thead');
  const tb=document.getElementById('nsl-kits-tbody');

  /* Sub-tabs */
  let th=`<div class="tab ${nslActiveKitTab==='all'?'active':''}" onclick="nsl_setKitTab('all')">All kits</div>`;
  KITS.forEach((k,i)=>{
    const out=nslKitParts.filter(x=>nsl_kitQtyStatus(x,i)==='out').length;
    const low=nslKitParts.filter(x=>nsl_kitQtyStatus(x,i)==='low').length;
    th+=`<div class="tab ${nslActiveKitTab==i?'active':''}" onclick="nsl_setKitTab(${i})">
      <span class="team-dot" style="background:${k.color}"></span>${k.name}
      ${out>0?`<span class="badge bd">${out}</span>`:low>0?`<span class="badge bw">${low}</span>`:''}
    </div>`;
  });
  document.getElementById('nsl-kits-tabs').innerHTML=th;

  const filtered=nslKitParts.filter(i=>{
    if(nslActiveKitTab!=='all'){
      const ki=+nslActiveKitTab;
      const st=nsl_kitQtyStatus(i,ki);
      if(fs==='ok'&&st!=='ok')return false;
      if(fs==='low'&&st!=='low')return false;
    } else {
      const ws=nsl_worstStatus(i.qtys.map((_,ki)=>nsl_kitQtyStatus(i,ki)));
      if(fs==='ok'&&ws!=='ok')return false;
      if(fs==='low'&&ws!=='low')return false;
    }
    if(fc&&i.cat!==fc)return false;
    if(s&&!i.name.toLowerCase().includes(s)&&!i.sku.toLowerCase().includes(s))return false;
    return true;
  });

  if(nslActiveKitTab==='all'){
    hint.innerHTML='<span><strong>All kits — overview.</strong> Select a kit tab to take inventory or top up.</span>';
    hint.style.cssText='font-size:11px;color:#888;margin-bottom:.625rem;padding:7px 11px;background:#f9f9f7;border-radius:7px;border:1px solid #e5e5e3;display:flex;align-items:center;justify-content:space-between;gap:10px;flex-wrap:wrap;';
    thead.innerHTML=`<tr>
      <th style="width:20%">Part name</th>
      <th style="width:9%">Bin #</th>
      <th style="width:9%">Category</th>
      <th style="width:8%"><span style="display:inline-flex;align-items:center;gap:2px"><span style="width:7px;height:7px;border-radius:50%;background:#0F9D58;display:inline-block"></span>Green</span></th>
      <th style="width:8%"><span style="display:inline-flex;align-items:center;gap:2px"><span style="width:7px;height:7px;border-radius:50%;background:#A32D2D;display:inline-block"></span>Red</span></th>
      <th style="width:8%"><span style="display:inline-flex;align-items:center;gap:2px"><span style="width:7px;height:7px;border-radius:50%;background:#BA7517;display:inline-block"></span>Yellow</span></th>
      <th style="width:8%"><span style="display:inline-flex;align-items:center;gap:2px"><span style="width:7px;height:7px;border-radius:50%;background:#D85A30;display:inline-block"></span>Orange</span></th>
      <th style="width:7%">Req/kit</th>
      <th style="width:10%">Have / Need</th>
      <th style="width:13%">Shortfall by kit</th>
    </tr>`;
    if(!filtered.length){tb.innerHTML='<tr><td colspan="10" style="text-align:center;padding:2rem;color:#888">No parts found</td></tr>';return;}
    tb.innerHTML=filtered.map(item=>{
      const totalHave=item.qtys.reduce((a,b)=>a+b,0);
      const req=item.reqQty;
      const totalShort=Math.max(0,req*4-totalHave);
      const fullyStocked=totalShort===0;
      const kitShorts=item.qtys.map((q,ki)=>({short:Math.max(0,req-q),color:KITS[ki].color})).filter(x=>x.short>0);
      const ws=nsl_worstStatus(item.qtys.map((_,ki)=>nsl_kitQtyStatus(item,ki)));
      const qCells=item.qtys.map((q,ki)=>{
        const st=nsl_kitQtyStatus(item,ki);
        const c=st==='out'?'color:#721c24':st==='low'?'color:#856404':'color:#1a1a1a';
        return`<td style="text-align:center;font-size:13px;font-weight:500;${c}">${q}</td>`;
      }).join('');
      const hvCell=fullyStocked
        ?`<span style="color:#155724;font-weight:600">${totalHave}</span> <span style="color:#aaa;font-size:10px">/ full</span>`
        :`<span style="font-weight:500">${totalHave}</span> <span style="color:#721c24;font-weight:600;font-size:12px"> / −${totalShort}</span>`;
      const sfCell=fullyStocked
        ?`<span style="color:#155724;font-size:11px">✓ All stocked</span>`
        :kitShorts.map(x=>`<span style="display:inline-flex;align-items:center;gap:2px;margin-right:4px;font-size:11px;color:#721c24;font-weight:600"><span style="width:7px;height:7px;border-radius:50%;background:${x.color};display:inline-block"></span>−${x.short}</span>`).join('');
      return`<tr class="${ws==='out'?'row-out':ws==='low'?'row-low':''}">
        <td style="font-weight:500" title="${nsl_esc(item.name)}">${item.name}</td>
        <td style="font-family:monospace;font-size:10px;color:#888">${item.sku}</td>
        <td style="color:#888;font-size:11px">${item.cat}</td>
        ${qCells}
        <td style="text-align:center;color:#666;font-weight:500">${req}</td>
        <td style="white-space:nowrap">${hvCell}</td>
        <td>${sfCell}</td>
      </tr>`;
    }).join('');
  } else {
    const ki=+nslActiveKitTab;
    const k=KITS[ki];
    hint.innerHTML=`
      <span><strong style="color:${k.color}">${k.name} kit — taking inventory.</strong> Use + / − to count what's physically in this kit.</span>
      <button class="btn btn-sm" style="background:${k.color};color:#fff;border-color:${k.color};white-space:nowrap;" onclick="nsl_openTopup('kit',${ki})">
        <svg width="11" height="11" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2.5"><polyline points="17 11 12 6 7 11"/><line x1="12" y1="18" x2="12" y2="6"/></svg>
        Top up ${k.name} kit
      </button>`;
    hint.style.cssText=`font-size:11px;color:#888;margin-bottom:.625rem;padding:7px 11px;background:${k.light};border-radius:7px;border:1px solid ${k.color}44;display:flex;align-items:center;justify-content:space-between;gap:10px;flex-wrap:wrap;`;
    thead.innerHTML=`<tr>
      <th style="width:33%">Part name</th>
      <th style="width:13%">Bin #</th>
      <th style="width:14%">Category</th>
      <th style="width:20%">Qty — <span style="color:${k.color};font-weight:600">${k.name}</span></th>
      <th style="width:11%">Required</th>
      <th style="width:9%">Status</th>
    </tr>`;
    if(!filtered.length){tb.innerHTML='<tr><td colspan="6" style="text-align:center;padding:2rem;color:#888">No parts found</td></tr>';return;}
    tb.innerHTML=filtered.map(item=>{
      const q=item.qtys[ki];
      const st=nsl_kitQtyStatus(item,ki);
      const qc=st==='out'?'color:#721c24':st==='low'?'color:#856404':'';
      return`<tr class="${st==='out'?'row-out':st==='low'?'row-low':''}">
        <td style="font-weight:500" title="${nsl_esc(item.name)}">${item.name}</td>
        <td style="font-family:monospace;font-size:10px;color:#888">${item.sku}</td>
        <td style="color:#888;font-size:11px">${item.cat}</td>
        <td><div class="qty-ctrl">
          <button class="qb" onclick="nsl_kitChgQty(${item.id},-1,${ki})">−</button>
          <span class="qn" style="${qc}">${q}</span>
          <button class="qb" onclick="nsl_kitChgQty(${item.id},1,${ki})">+</button>
        </div></td>
        <td style="color:#666">${item.reqQty}</td>
        <td>${nsl_badge(st)}</td>
      </tr>`;
    }).join('');
  }
}
function nsl_setKitTab(t){nslActiveKitTab=t;nsl_renderKits();}
function nsl_kitChgQty(id,d,ki){
  const it=nslKitParts.find(x=>x.id===id);
  if(it){it.qtys[ki]=Math.max(0,it.qtys[ki]+d);nsl_renderKits();if(nslActivePage==='master')nsl_renderMaster();persistNslKitPart(it);}
}

/* ═══════════════════════════════════
   WORKSTATIONS PAGE
════════════════════════════════════ */
function nsl_renderWorkstations(){
  const s=document.getElementById('nsl-ws-srch').value.toLowerCase();
  const fc=document.getElementById('nsl-ws-fcat').value;
  const fs=document.getElementById('nsl-ws-fstk').value;
  const hint=document.getElementById('nsl-ws-hint');
  const thead=document.getElementById('nsl-ws-thead');
  const tb=document.getElementById('nsl-ws-tbody');

  /* Sub-tabs */
  let th=`<div class="tab ${nslActiveWsTab==='all'?'active':''}" onclick="nsl_setWsTab('all')">All workstations</div>`;
  WORKSTATIONS.forEach((w,i)=>{
    const out=nslWsParts.filter(x=>nsl_wsQtyStatus(x,i)==='out').length;
    const low=nslWsParts.filter(x=>nsl_wsQtyStatus(x,i)==='low').length;
    th+=`<div class="tab ${nslActiveWsTab==i?'active':''}" onclick="nsl_setWsTab(${i})">
      <span class="team-dot" style="background:${w.color}"></span>${w.name}
      ${out>0?`<span class="badge bd">${out}</span>`:low>0?`<span class="badge bw">${low}</span>`:''}
    </div>`;
  });
  document.getElementById('nsl-ws-tabs').innerHTML=th;

  const filtered=nslWsParts.filter(i=>{
    if(nslActiveWsTab!=='all'){
      const wi=+nslActiveWsTab;
      const st=nsl_wsQtyStatus(i,wi);
      if(fs==='ok'&&st!=='ok')return false;
      if(fs==='low'&&st!=='low')return false;
    } else {
      const ws=nsl_worstStatus(i.qtys.map((_,wi)=>nsl_wsQtyStatus(i,wi)));
      if(fs==='ok'&&ws!=='ok')return false;
      if(fs==='low'&&ws!=='low')return false;
    }
    if(fc&&i.cat!==fc)return false;
    if(s&&!i.name.toLowerCase().includes(s)&&!i.sku.toLowerCase().includes(s))return false;
    return true;
  });

  if(nslActiveWsTab==='all'){
    hint.innerHTML='<span><strong>All workstations — overview.</strong> Select a workstation tab to take inventory or top up.</span>';
    hint.style.cssText='font-size:11px;color:#888;margin-bottom:.625rem;padding:7px 11px;background:#f9f9f7;border-radius:7px;border:1px solid #e5e5e3;display:flex;align-items:center;justify-content:space-between;gap:10px;flex-wrap:wrap;';
    thead.innerHTML=`<tr>
      <th style="width:24%">Item name</th>
      <th style="width:10%">Bin #</th>
      <th style="width:12%">Category</th>
      <th style="width:12%"><span style="display:inline-flex;align-items:center;gap:3px"><span style="width:7px;height:7px;border-radius:50%;background:#534AB7;display:inline-block"></span>Classroom</span></th>
      <th style="width:12%"><span style="display:inline-flex;align-items:center;gap:3px"><span style="width:7px;height:7px;border-radius:50%;background:#0F6E56;display:inline-block"></span>Portable</span></th>
      <th style="width:7%">Req/stn</th>
      <th style="width:10%">Have / Need</th>
      <th style="width:13%">Shortfall</th>
    </tr>`;
    if(!filtered.length){tb.innerHTML='<tr><td colspan="8" style="text-align:center;padding:2rem;color:#888">No items found</td></tr>';return;}
    tb.innerHTML=filtered.map(item=>{
      const totalHave=item.qtys.reduce((a,b)=>a+b,0);
      const req=item.reqQty;
      const totalShort=Math.max(0,req*2-totalHave);
      const fullyStocked=totalShort===0;
      const wsShorts=item.qtys.map((q,wi)=>({short:Math.max(0,req-q),color:WORKSTATIONS[wi].color,name:WORKSTATIONS[wi].name})).filter(x=>x.short>0);
      const ws=nsl_worstStatus(item.qtys.map((_,wi)=>nsl_wsQtyStatus(item,wi)));
      const qCells=item.qtys.map((q,wi)=>{
        const st=nsl_wsQtyStatus(item,wi);
        const c=st==='out'?'color:#721c24':st==='low'?'color:#856404':'color:#1a1a1a';
        return`<td style="text-align:center;font-size:13px;font-weight:500;${c}">${q}</td>`;
      }).join('');
      const hvCell=fullyStocked
        ?`<span style="color:#155724;font-weight:600">${totalHave}</span> <span style="color:#aaa;font-size:10px">/ full</span>`
        :`<span style="font-weight:500">${totalHave}</span> <span style="color:#721c24;font-weight:600;font-size:12px"> / −${totalShort}</span>`;
      const sfCell=fullyStocked
        ?`<span style="color:#155724;font-size:11px">✓ Both stocked</span>`
        :wsShorts.map(x=>`<span style="display:inline-flex;align-items:center;gap:2px;margin-right:4px;font-size:11px;color:#721c24;font-weight:600"><span style="width:7px;height:7px;border-radius:50%;background:${x.color};display:inline-block"></span>−${x.short}</span>`).join('');
      return`<tr class="${ws==='out'?'row-out':ws==='low'?'row-low':''}">
        <td style="font-weight:500" title="${nsl_esc(item.name)}">${item.name}</td>
        <td style="font-family:monospace;font-size:10px;color:#888">${item.sku}</td>
        <td style="color:#888;font-size:11px">${item.cat}</td>
        ${qCells}
        <td style="text-align:center;color:#666;font-weight:500">${req}</td>
        <td style="white-space:nowrap">${hvCell}</td>
        <td>${sfCell}</td>
      </tr>`;
    }).join('');
  } else {
    const wi=+nslActiveWsTab;
    const w=WORKSTATIONS[wi];
    hint.innerHTML=`
      <span><strong style="color:${w.color}">${w.name} workstation — taking inventory.</strong> Use + / − to count what's physically at this workstation.</span>
      <button class="btn btn-sm" style="background:${w.color};color:#fff;border-color:${w.color};white-space:nowrap;" onclick="nsl_openTopup('ws',${wi})">
        <svg width="11" height="11" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2.5"><polyline points="17 11 12 6 7 11"/><line x1="12" y1="18" x2="12" y2="6"/></svg>
        Top up ${w.name}
      </button>`;
    hint.style.cssText=`font-size:11px;color:#888;margin-bottom:.625rem;padding:7px 11px;background:${w.light};border-radius:7px;border:1px solid ${w.color}44;display:flex;align-items:center;justify-content:space-between;gap:10px;flex-wrap:wrap;`;
    thead.innerHTML=`<tr>
      <th style="width:24%">Item name</th>
      <th style="width:10%">Bin #</th>
      <th style="width:11%">Category</th>
      <th style="width:14%">New qty — <span style="color:${w.color};font-weight:600">${w.name}</span></th>
      <th style="width:12%">Used — serviceable</th>
      <th style="width:12%">Used — repair</th>
      <th style="width:9%">Required</th>
      <th style="width:8%">Status</th>
    </tr>`;
    if(!filtered.length){tb.innerHTML='<tr><td colspan="8" style="text-align:center;padding:2rem;color:#888">No items found</td></tr>';return;}
    tb.innerHTML=filtered.map(item=>{
      const q=item.qtys[wi];
      const st=nsl_wsQtyStatus(item,wi);
      const qc=st==='out'?'color:#721c24':st==='low'?'color:#856404':'';
      const wug=item.wsUsedGood||0;
      const wur=item.wsUsedRepair||0;
      return`<tr class="${st==='out'?'row-out':st==='low'?'row-low':''}">
        <td style="font-weight:500" title="${nsl_esc(item.name)}">${item.name}</td>
        <td style="font-family:monospace;font-size:10px;color:#888">${item.sku}</td>
        <td style="color:#888;font-size:11px">${item.cat}</td>
        <td><div class="qty-ctrl">
          <button class="qb" onclick="nsl_wsChgQty(${item.id},-1,${wi})">−</button>
          <span class="qn" style="${qc}">${q}</span>
          <button class="qb" onclick="nsl_wsChgQty(${item.id},1,${wi})">+</button>
        </div></td>
        <td><div class="qty-ctrl">
          <button class="qb" onclick="nsl_wsChgUsed(${item.id},'good',-1)">−</button>
          <span class="qn" style="${wug>0?'color:#185FA5':''}">${wug}</span>
          <button class="qb" onclick="nsl_wsChgUsed(${item.id},'good',1)">+</button>
        </div></td>
        <td><div class="qty-ctrl">
          <button class="qb" onclick="nsl_wsChgUsed(${item.id},'repair',-1)">−</button>
          <span class="qn" style="${wur>0?'color:#856404':''}">${wur}</span>
          <button class="qb" onclick="nsl_wsChgUsed(${item.id},'repair',1)">+</button>
        </div></td>
        <td style="color:#666">${item.reqQty}</td>
        <td>${nsl_badge(st)}</td>
      </tr>`;
    }).join('');
  }
}
function nsl_setWsTab(t){nslActiveWsTab=t;nsl_renderWorkstations();}
function nsl_wsChgQty(id,d,wi){
  const it=nslWsParts.find(x=>x.id===id);
  if(it){it.qtys[wi]=Math.max(0,it.qtys[wi]+d);nsl_renderWorkstations();if(nslActivePage==='master')nsl_renderMaster();persistNslWsPart(it);}
}
function nsl_wsChgUsed(id,type,d){
  const it=nslWsParts.find(x=>x.id===id);
  if(!it)return;
  if(type==='good')it.wsUsedGood=Math.max(0,(it.wsUsedGood||0)+d);
  else it.wsUsedRepair=Math.max(0,(it.wsUsedRepair||0)+d);
  nsl_renderWorkstations();if(nslActivePage==='master')nsl_renderMaster();persistNslWsPart(it);
}

/* ═══════════════════════════════════
   TOP-UP MODAL — shared for kits & workstations
════════════════════════════════════ */
function nsl_openTopup(type,idx){
  nslTopupMode={type,idx};
  const isKit=type==='kit';
  const loc=isKit?KITS[idx]:WORKSTATIONS[idx];
  const parts=isKit?nslKitParts:nslWsParts;
  const shortItems=parts.filter(i=>i.qtys[idx]<i.reqQty);
  document.getElementById('nsl-topup-title').textContent=`Top up — ${loc.name} ${isKit?'kit':'workstation'}`;
  const body=document.getElementById('nsl-topup-body');
  if(!shortItems.length){
    body.innerHTML=`<div style="text-align:center;padding:2rem;color:#155724;font-weight:500;background:#E8F5E9;border-radius:8px;">
      <div style="font-size:24px;margin-bottom:.5rem">✓</div>
      ${loc.name} ${isKit?'kit':'workstation'} is fully stocked — nothing to top up!
    </div>`;
    document.getElementById('nsl-topup-confirm-btn').style.display='none';
  } else {
    document.getElementById('nsl-topup-confirm-btn').style.display='inline-flex';
    body.innerHTML=shortItems.map(item=>{
      const need=item.reqQty-item.qtys[idx];
      const avail=item.srQty;
      const suggested=Math.min(need,avail);
      const cantFull=avail<need;
      return`<div class="topup-item${cantFull?' warn':''}">
        <div class="topup-item-name">${item.name} <span style="font-family:monospace;font-size:10px;font-weight:400;color:#888">${item.sku}</span></div>
        <div class="topup-stats">
          <span>Has: <strong>${item.qtys[idx]}</strong></span>
          <span>Required: <strong>${item.reqQty}</strong></span>
          <span>Needs: <strong style="color:#856404">+${need}</strong></span>
          <span>SR new stock: <strong style="${avail===0?'color:#721c24':''}">${avail}</strong></span>
        </div>
        ${cantFull?`<div class="topup-warn">⚠ Stock room only has ${avail} — will still be ${need-avail} short after transfer${avail===0?' (none available)':''}.</div>`:''}
        <div class="topup-transfer">
          <label>Transfer from stock room (new stock):</label>
          <input type="number" min="0" max="${avail}" value="${suggested}" id="tt-${item.id}" ${avail===0?'disabled':''}/>
          <span style="color:#888;font-size:11px">of ${avail} available</span>
        </div>
      </div>`;
    }).join('');
  }
  document.getElementById('nsl-topup-overlay').classList.add('open');
}
function nsl_closeTopup(){
  document.getElementById('nsl-topup-overlay').classList.remove('open');
  nslTopupMode=null;
}
function nsl_confirmTopup(){
  if(!nslTopupMode) return;
  const {type,idx}=nslTopupMode;
  const isKit=type==='kit';
  const loc=isKit?KITS[idx]:WORKSTATIONS[idx];
  const parts=isKit?nslKitParts:nslWsParts;
  const shortItems=parts.filter(i=>i.qtys[idx]<i.reqQty);
  let moved=0,warnings=0;
  shortItems.forEach(item=>{
    const inp=document.getElementById('tt-'+item.id);
    if(!inp||inp.disabled)return;
    const transfer=Math.min(Math.max(0,parseInt(inp.value)||0),item.srQty);
    if(transfer>0){
      item.qtys[idx]+=transfer;
      /* Sync srQty across all items sharing this SKU */
      nsl_syncSrQtyBySku(item.sku,item.srQty-transfer);
      moved++;
      if(item.qtys[idx]<item.reqQty)warnings++;
    }
  });
  nsl_closeTopup();
  nsl_renderAllViews();
  if(moved===0){nsl_toast('No items transferred');return;}
  if(warnings>0)nsl_toast(`${loc.name} topped up — ${warnings} item${warnings>1?'s':''} still below required`,4000);
  else nsl_toast(`${loc.name} fully topped up ✓`);
}

/* ═══════════════════════════════════
   STOCK ROOM PAGE
════════════════════════════════════ */
function nsl_renderStockRoom(){
  const s=document.getElementById('nsl-sr-srch').value.toLowerCase();
  const fc=document.getElementById('nsl-sr-fcat').value;
  const fs=document.getElementById('nsl-sr-fstk').value;
  /* Build merged unique-SKU list */
  const srItems=nsl_buildSrItems();
  const filtered=srItems.filter(i=>{
    const st=nsl_srStatus(i.srQty,i.srMin);
    if(fs==='ok'&&st!=='ok')return false;
    if(fs==='low'&&st==='ok')return false;
    if(fc&&i.cat!==fc)return false;
    if(s&&!i.name.toLowerCase().includes(s)&&!i.sku.toLowerCase().includes(s))return false;
    return true;
  });
  const tb=document.getElementById('nsl-sr-tbody');
  if(!filtered.length){tb.innerHTML='<tr><td colspan="8" style="text-align:center;padding:2rem;color:#888">No items found</td></tr>';return;}
  tb.innerHTML=filtered.map(item=>{
    const st=nsl_srStatus(item.srQty,item.srMin);
    const qc=st==='out'?'color:#721c24':st==='low'?'color:#856404':'';
    const ug=item.srUsedGood||0;
    const ur=item.srUsedRepair||0;
    return`<tr class="${st==='out'?'row-out':st==='low'?'row-low':''}">
      <td style="font-weight:500" title="${nsl_esc(item.name)}">${item.name}</td>
      <td style="font-family:monospace;font-size:10px;color:#888">${item.sku}</td>
      <td style="color:#888;font-size:11px">${item.cat}</td>
      <td><div class="qty-ctrl">
        <button class="qb" onclick="nsl_srChgQty('${item.sku}','new',-1)">−</button>
        <span class="qn" style="${qc}">${item.srQty}</span>
        <button class="qb" onclick="nsl_srChgQty('${item.sku}','new',1)">+</button>
      </div></td>
      <td><div class="qty-ctrl">
        <button class="qb" onclick="nsl_srChgQty('${item.sku}','usedGood',-1)">−</button>
        <span class="qn" style="${ug>0?'color:#185FA5':''}">${ug}</span>
        <button class="qb" onclick="nsl_srChgQty('${item.sku}','usedGood',1)">+</button>
      </div></td>
      <td><div class="qty-ctrl">
        <button class="qb" onclick="nsl_srChgQty('${item.sku}','usedRepair',-1)">−</button>
        <span class="qn" style="${ur>0?'color:#856404':''}">${ur}</span>
        <button class="qb" onclick="nsl_srChgQty('${item.sku}','usedRepair',1)">+</button>
      </div></td>
      <td style="color:#666;text-align:center;">${item.srMin}</td>
      <td>${nsl_badge(st)}</td>
    </tr>`;
  }).join('');
}
function nsl_srChgQty(sku,field,d){
  const cur=nslKitParts.find(i=>i.sku===sku)||nslWsParts.find(i=>i.sku===sku);
  if(!cur)return;
  if(field==='new'){nsl_syncSrQtyBySku(sku,Math.max(0,cur.srQty+d));}
  else if(field==='usedGood'){nsl_syncSrUsedGoodBySku(sku,Math.max(0,(cur.srUsedGood||0)+d));}
  else if(field==='usedRepair'){nsl_syncSrUsedRepairBySku(sku,Math.max(0,(cur.srUsedRepair||0)+d));}
  nsl_renderStockRoom();
  if(nslActivePage==='master')nsl_renderMaster();
  nslKitParts.filter(i=>i.sku===sku).forEach(persistNslKitPart);
  nslWsParts.filter(i=>i.sku===sku).forEach(persistNslWsPart);
}

/* ═══════════════════════════════════
   MASTER STOCK PAGE
════════════════════════════════════ */
function nsl_renderMaster(){
  const s=document.getElementById('nsl-master-srch').value.toLowerCase();
  const fc=document.getElementById('nsl-master-fcat').value;
  const fs=document.getElementById('nsl-master-fstk').value;
  /* Build unified master list: merge kit parts and ws parts by SKU */
  const masterMap=new Map();
  nslKitParts.forEach(item=>{
    const inKits=item.qtys.reduce((a,b)=>a+b,0);
    if(!masterMap.has(item.sku)){
      masterMap.set(item.sku,{
        name:item.name,sku:item.sku,cat:item.cat,
        srQty:item.srQty,srMin:item.srMin,
        srUsedGood:item.srUsedGood||0,srUsedRepair:item.srUsedRepair||0,
        inKits,inWs:0,wsUsedGood:0,wsUsedRepair:0,
        kitReq:item.reqQty*4,wsReq:0
      });
    } else {
      const ex=masterMap.get(item.sku);
      ex.inKits+=inKits;
      ex.kitReq+=item.reqQty*4;
    }
  });
  nslWsParts.forEach(item=>{
    const inWs=item.qtys.reduce((a,b)=>a+b,0);
    if(!masterMap.has(item.sku)){
      masterMap.set(item.sku,{
        name:item.name,sku:item.sku,cat:item.cat,
        srQty:item.srQty,srMin:item.srMin,
        srUsedGood:item.srUsedGood||0,srUsedRepair:item.srUsedRepair||0,
        inKits:0,inWs,wsUsedGood:item.wsUsedGood||0,wsUsedRepair:item.wsUsedRepair||0,
        kitReq:0,wsReq:item.reqQty*2
      });
    } else {
      const ex=masterMap.get(item.sku);
      ex.inWs+=inWs;
      ex.wsReq+=item.reqQty*2;
      ex.srMin=Math.max(ex.srMin,item.srMin);
      ex.srUsedGood=Math.max(ex.srUsedGood,item.srUsedGood||0);
      ex.srUsedRepair=Math.max(ex.srUsedRepair,item.srUsedRepair||0);
      ex.wsUsedGood+=(item.wsUsedGood||0);
      ex.wsUsedRepair+=(item.wsUsedRepair||0);
    }
  });
  const allItems=Array.from(masterMap.values());
  const filtered=allItems.filter(i=>{
    const srUG=i.srUsedGood||0;
    const wsUG=i.wsUsedGood||0;
    const totalAvail=i.srQty+i.inKits+i.inWs+srUG+wsUG;
    const totalReq=i.kitReq+i.wsReq;
    const shortfall=Math.max(0,totalReq-totalAvail);
    if(fs==='low'&&shortfall===0)return false;
    if(fc&&i.cat!==fc)return false;
    if(s&&!i.name.toLowerCase().includes(s)&&!i.sku.toLowerCase().includes(s))return false;
    return true;
  });
  const tb=document.getElementById('nsl-master-tbody');
  if(!filtered.length){tb.innerHTML='<tr><td colspan="14" style="text-align:center;padding:2rem;color:#888">No items found</td></tr>';return;}
  tb.innerHTML=filtered.map(item=>{
    const srUG=item.srUsedGood||0;
    const srUR=item.srUsedRepair||0;
    const wsUG=item.wsUsedGood||0;
    const totalAvail=item.srQty+item.inKits+item.inWs+srUG+wsUG;
    const totalReq=item.kitReq+item.wsReq;
    const shortfall=Math.max(0,totalReq-totalAvail);
    const srSt=nsl_srStatus(item.srQty,item.srMin);
    const overallSt=shortfall>0?(shortfall>=totalReq?'out':'low'):'ok';
    return`<tr class="${overallSt==='out'?'row-out':overallSt==='low'?'row-low':''}">
      <td style="font-weight:500" title="${nsl_esc(item.name)}">${item.name}</td>
      <td style="font-family:monospace;font-size:10px;color:#888">${item.sku}</td>
      <td style="color:#888;font-size:11px">${item.cat}</td>
      <td style="text-align:center;font-weight:500">${item.srQty}</td>
      <td style="text-align:center;color:#185FA5;font-weight:500">${srUG||'—'}</td>
      <td style="text-align:center;color:#856404;font-weight:500">${srUR||'—'}</td>
      <td style="text-align:center;color:#666">${item.inKits}</td>
      <td style="text-align:center;color:#666">${item.inWs}</td>
      <td style="text-align:center;color:#185FA5">${wsUG||'—'}</td>
      <td style="text-align:center;font-weight:600">${totalAvail}</td>
      <td style="text-align:center;color:#666">${totalReq||'—'}</td>
      <td style="text-align:center;font-weight:600;${shortfall>0?'color:#721c24':'color:#155724'}">${shortfall>0?'−'+shortfall:'✓'}</td>
      <td style="text-align:center;${srSt==='out'?'color:#721c24':srSt==='low'?'color:#856404':'color:#155724'}">${item.srMin}</td>
      <td>${nsl_badge(srSt)}</td>
    </tr>`;
  }).join('');
}

/* ═══════════════════════════════════
   RENDER ALL
════════════════════════════════════ */
function nsl_renderAllViews(){
  if(nslActivePage==='kits')nsl_renderKits();
  else if(nslActivePage==='workstations')nsl_renderWorkstations();
  else if(nslActivePage==='stockroom')nsl_renderStockRoom();
  else if(nslActivePage==='master')nsl_renderMaster();
}

/* ═══════════════════════════════════
   CSV / DRIVE
════════════════════════════════════ */
function nsl_getCSV(){
  const kHeader=['Type','Part/Item Name','Bin #','Category','Req Qty','Green','Red','Yellow','Orange','Classroom','Portable','SR Qty','SR Min Qty'];
  const kRows=nslKitParts.map(i=>['Kit Part',i.name,i.sku,i.cat,i.reqQty,...i.qtys,'','',i.srQty,i.srMin]);
  const wRows=nslWsParts.map(i=>['WS Item',i.name,i.sku,i.cat,i.reqQty,'','','','', ...i.qtys,i.srQty,i.srMin]);
  return[kHeader,...kRows,...wRows].map(r=>r.map(c=>`"${c}"`).join(',')).join('\n');
}
function nsl_localCSV(){
  const a=document.createElement('a');
  a.href='data:text/csv;charset=utf-8,'+encodeURIComponent(getCSV());
  // REMOVED: a.download=document.getElementById('nsl-fname').value||'NSL_Inventory_Dashboard.csv';
  a.click();nsl_toast('CSV downloaded');
}
async function nsl_saveToDrive(){
  // REMOVED: const btn=document.getElementById('nsl-save-btn');
  const msg=document.getElementById('nsl-sync-msg');
  const fname=document.getElementById('nsl-fname').value.trim()||'NSL_Inventory_Dashboard.csv';
  btn.disabled=true;btn.textContent='Saving…';msg.textContent='';
  const updated=new Date().toLocaleString();
  try{
    const res=await fetch("https://api.anthropic.com/v1/messages",{method:"POST",headers:{"Content-Type":"application/json"},
      body:JSON.stringify({model:"claude-sonnet-4-20250514",max_tokens:1000,
        mcp_servers:[{type:"url",url:"https://gcal.mcp.claude.com/mcp",name:"gcal"},{type:"url",url:"https://gmail.mcp.claude.com/mcp",name:"gmail"}],
        messages:[{role:"user",content:`Save CSV as "${fname}" in Google Drive (replace if exists). Updated ${updated}.\n\n${getCSV()}\n\nConfirm with link.`}]})});
    const data=await res.json();
    const text=(data.content||[]).filter(b=>b.type==='text').map(b=>b.text).join('\n');
    const urlMatch=text.match(/https:\/\/drive\.google\.com\/[^\s)"<]+/);
    if(urlMatch){document.getElementById('nsl-drive-status').innerHTML=`Saved ${updated} — <a href="${urlMatch[0]}" target="_blank" style="color:#185FA5">Open ↗</a>`;msg.textContent='Saved ✓';nsl_toast('Saved to Drive ✓');}
    else if(/saved|created|uploaded|success/i.test(text)){document.getElementById('nsl-drive-status').textContent=`Saved: ${updated}`;msg.textContent='Saved ✓';nsl_toast('Saved to Drive ✓');}
    else{nsl_toast('Drive write unavailable — use ↓ CSV',4000);}
  }catch(e){nsl_toast('Error — use ↓ CSV',4000);}
  btn.disabled=false;
  btn.innerHTML='<svg width="12" height="12" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2.5"><polyline points="22 12 16 12 14 15 10 15 8 12 2 12"/><path d="M5.45 5.11L2 12v6a2 2 0 002 2h16a2 2 0 002-2v-6l-3.45-6.89A2 2 0 0016.76 4H7.24a2 2 0 00-1.79 1.11z"/></svg> Save to Drive';
}
async function nsl_loadFromDrive(){
  const msg=document.getElementById('nsl-sync-msg');
  const fname=document.getElementById('nsl-fname').value.trim()||'NSL_Inventory_Dashboard.csv';
  msg.textContent='Loading…';
  try{
    const res=await fetch("https://api.anthropic.com/v1/messages",{method:"POST",headers:{"Content-Type":"application/json"},
      body:JSON.stringify({model:"claude-sonnet-4-20250514",max_tokens:4000,
        mcp_servers:[{type:"url",url:"https://gcal.mcp.claude.com/mcp",name:"gcal"},{type:"url",url:"https://gmail.mcp.claude.com/mcp",name:"gmail"}],
        messages:[{role:"user",content:`Read file "${fname}" from Google Drive. Return ONLY raw CSV, no markdown.`}]})});
    const data=await res.json();
    const text=(data.content||[]).filter(b=>b.type==='text').map(b=>b.text).join('\n').trim();
    const lines=text.split('\n').filter(l=>l.trim());
    if(lines.length>1){
      nsl_parseAndLoad(lines);
      nsl_renderAllViews();msg.textContent='Loaded ✓';nsl_toast('Data loaded from Drive ✓');
    }else{msg.textContent='Not found';nsl_toast('"'+fname+'" not found',4000);}
  }catch(e){msg.textContent='Error';}
}
function nsl_parseAndLoad(lines){
  const newKit=[],newWs=[];
  let ki=1,wi=1;
  for(let i=1;i<lines.length;i++){
    const c=lines[i].split(',').map(x=>x.replace(/^"|"$/g,'').trim());
    if(c.length<13)continue;
    const type=c[0],name=c[1],sku=c[2],cat=c[3];
    const req=parseInt(c[4])||1;
    if(type==='Kit Part'){
      newKit.push({id:ki++,name,sku,cat,reqQty:req,
        qtys:[parseInt(c[5])||0,parseInt(c[6])||0,parseInt(c[7])||0,parseInt(c[8])||0],
        srQty:parseInt(c[11])||0,srMin:parseInt(c[12])||1});
    } else if(type==='WS Item'){
      newWs.push({id:wi++,name,sku,cat,reqQty:req,
        qtys:[parseInt(c[9])||0,parseInt(c[10])||0],
        srQty:parseInt(c[11])||0,srMin:parseInt(c[12])||1});
    }
  }
  if(newKit.length)nslKitParts=newKit;
  if(newWs.length)nslWsParts=newWs;
  nslNextKitId=nslKitParts.length+100;
  nslNextWsId=nslWsParts.length+200;
}
