/* ═══════════════════════════════════
   UTILITIES
════════════════════════════════════ */
function ecar_toast(msg,dur=2800){const el=document.getElementById('ecar-toast');el.textContent=msg;el.classList.add('show');setTimeout(()=>el.classList.remove('show'),dur);}
function ecar_esc(s){return(s||'').replace(/&/g,'&amp;').replace(/"/g,'&quot;').replace(/</g,'&lt;');}
function ecar_qStatus(q,req){if(q===0)return'out';if(q<req)return'low';return'ok';}
function ecar_srStatus(srQty,srMin){if(srQty===0)return'out';if(srQty<=srMin)return'low';return'ok';}
function ecar_trStatus(trQty,trMin){if(trQty===0)return'out';if(trQty<=trMin)return'low';return'ok';}
function ecar_worstOf(arr){if(arr.includes('out'))return'out';if(arr.includes('low'))return'low';return'ok';}
function ecar_badge(s){
  if(s==='ok')return'<span class="badge bs">OK</span>';
  if(s==='low')return'<span class="badge bw">Low</span>';
  return'<span class="badge bd">Out</span>';
}
function carIdxByName(name){return ALL_CARS.indexOf(name);}
function ecar_groupForCar(name){
  const g=GROUPS.find(g=>g.cars.includes(name));
  return g||null;
}
function ecar_partsForGroup(gid){
  if(gid==='gob')return ecarGobParts;
  return ecarHmsParts;
}
function ecar_carIndicesForGroup(gid){
  if(gid==='hs')return[0,1,2];
  if(gid==='ms')return[3,4,5];
  if(gid==='gob')return[0,1];
  return null;
}

function ecar_syncSrUsedGoodAcross(sku,qty){
  [ecarHmsParts,ecarGobParts,ecarWsParts].forEach(cat=>cat.filter(i=>i.sku===sku).forEach(i=>i.srUsedGood=qty));
}
function ecar_syncSrUsedRepairAcross(sku,qty){
  [ecarHmsParts,ecarGobParts,ecarWsParts].forEach(cat=>cat.filter(i=>i.sku===sku).forEach(i=>i.srUsedRepair=qty));
}
function ecar_syncTrUsedGoodAcross(sku,qty){
  [ecarHmsParts,ecarGobParts,ecarWsParts].forEach(cat=>cat.filter(i=>i.sku===sku).forEach(i=>i.trUsedGood=qty));
}
function ecar_syncTrUsedRepairAcross(sku,qty){
  [ecarHmsParts,ecarGobParts,ecarWsParts].forEach(cat=>cat.filter(i=>i.sku===sku).forEach(i=>i.trUsedRepair=qty));
}
function ecar_syncSrAcrossCatalogs(sku,qty){
  [ecarHmsParts,ecarGobParts,ecarWsParts].forEach(cat=>cat.filter(i=>i.sku===sku).forEach(i=>i.srQty=qty));
}
function ecar_syncSrMinAcrossCatalogs(sku,min){
  [ecarHmsParts,ecarGobParts,ecarWsParts].forEach(cat=>cat.filter(i=>i.sku===sku).forEach(i=>i.srMin=min));
}
function ecar_syncTrAcrossCatalogs(sku,qty){
  [ecarHmsParts,ecarGobParts,ecarWsParts].forEach(cat=>cat.filter(i=>i.sku===sku).forEach(i=>i.trQty=qty));
}
function ecar_getSrQtyBySku(sku){
  const all=[...ecarHmsParts,...ecarGobParts,...ecarWsParts];
  const f=all.find(i=>i.sku===sku);
  return f?{srQty:f.srQty,srMin:f.srMin,trQty:f.trQty}:{srQty:0,srMin:0,trQty:0};
}

function ecar_populateCatDropdowns(){
  const opts=ecarCategories.map(c=>`<option value="${ecar_esc(c)}">${ecar_esc(c)}</option>`).join('');
  const fOpts='<option value="">All categories</option>'+opts;
  ['ecar-cars-fcat','ecar-ws-fcat','ecar-tr-fcat','ecar-sr-fcat','ecar-master-fcat',
   'ecar-hf-cat','ecar-gf-cat','ecar-wf-cat','ecar-hp-fcat','ecar-gp-fcat','ecar-wp-fcat'].forEach(id=>{
    const el=document.getElementById(id);if(!el)return;
    const prev=el.value;
    const isFilter=['ecar-cars-fcat','ecar-ws-fcat','ecar-tr-fcat','ecar-sr-fcat','ecar-master-fcat','ecar-hp-fcat','ecar-gp-fcat','ecar-wp-fcat'].includes(id);
    el.innerHTML=isFilter?fOpts:opts;
    if(prev)el.value=prev;
  });
}

/* ═══════════════════════════════════
   PAGE NAV
════════════════════════════════════ */
function ecar_gotoPage(p){
  document.querySelectorAll('#ecar-module .page').forEach(x=>x.classList.remove('active'));
  document.querySelectorAll('#ecar-module .nav-tab').forEach(x=>x.classList.remove('active'));
  document.getElementById('ecar-page-'+p).classList.add('active');
  document.getElementById('ecar-nav-'+p).classList.add('active');
  ecarActivePage=p;
  if(p==='cars')ecar_renderCars();
  else if(p==='workspaces')ecar_renderWorkspaces();
  else if(p==='trailer')ecar_renderTrailer();
  else if(p==='stockroom')ecar_renderStockRoom();
  else if(p==='master')ecar_renderMaster();
  else if(p==='setup')ecar_renderSetup();
}

/* ═══════════════════════════════════
   ecarPassword
════════════════════════════════════ */
function ecar_clickSetup(){
  if(ecarSetupUnlocked){ecar_gotoPage('setup');return;}
  document.getElementById('ecar-pwd-input').value='';
  document.getElementById('ecar-pwd-err').textContent='';
  document.getElementById('ecar-pwd-overlay').classList.add('open');
  setTimeout(()=>document.getElementById('ecar-pwd-input').focus(),80);
}
function ecar_closePwd(){document.getElementById('ecar-pwd-overlay').classList.remove('open');}
function ecar_checkPwd(){
  const v=document.getElementById('ecar-pwd-input').value;
  if(v===ecarPassword){
    ecar_closePwd();ecarSetupUnlocked=true;
    document.getElementById('ecar-setup-locked-bar').style.display='none';
    document.getElementById('ecar-setup-content').style.display='block';
    document.getElementById('ecar-setup-tab-label').textContent='Setup ✓';
    ecar_gotoPage('setup');
  } else {
    const f=document.getElementById('ecar-pwd-input');
    f.classList.add('shake');
    document.getElementById('ecar-pwd-err').textContent='Incorrect password.';
    f.value='';
    setTimeout(()=>f.classList.remove('shake'),350);
  }
}
function ecar_lockSetup(){
  ecarSetupUnlocked=false;
  document.getElementById('ecar-setup-locked-bar').style.display='flex';
  document.getElementById('ecar-setup-content').style.display='none';
  document.getElementById('ecar-setup-tab-label').textContent='Setup';
  ecar_gotoPage('cars');ecar_toast('Setup locked');
}
function ecar_changePassword(){
  const p1=document.getElementById('ecar-np1').value.trim();
  const p2=document.getElementById('ecar-np2').value.trim();
  const msg=document.getElementById('ecar-pwd-msg');
  if(!p1){msg.style.color='#dc3545';msg.textContent='Cannot be empty.';return;}
  if(p1!==p2){msg.style.color='#dc3545';msg.textContent='Passwords do not match.';return;}
  if(p1.length<3){msg.style.color='#dc3545';msg.textContent='Min 3 characters.';return;}
  ecarPassword=p1;
  document.getElementById('ecar-np1').value='';document.getElementById('ecar-np2').value='';
  msg.style.color='#2E7D32';msg.textContent='Password updated ✓';
  setTimeout(()=>msg.textContent='',3000);ecar_toast('Password changed ✓');
}

/* ═══════════════════════════════════
   CATEGORIES
════════════════════════════════════ */
const ECAR_DEFAULT_CATS=['Drivetrain','Suspension','Body & Chassis','Electronics','Tires & Wheels','Fasteners','Consumables'];
function ecar_renderCatList(){
  document.getElementById('ecar-cat-list').innerHTML=ecarCategories.map(c=>`
    <span class="cat-pill">${ecar_esc(c)}${!ECAR_DEFAULT_CATS.includes(c)?`<span class="cat-del" onclick="ecar_deleteCategory('${ecar_esc(c)}')" title="Remove">×</span>`:''}</span>`).join('');
}
function ecar_addCategory(){
  const inp=document.getElementById('ecar-new-cat');
  const name=inp.value.trim();
  if(!name)return;
  if(ecarCategories.includes(name)){ecar_toast('Already exists');return;}
  ecarCategories.push(name);inp.value='';
  ecar_renderCatList();ecar_populateCatDropdowns();ecar_toast(`"${name}" added`);
}
function ecar_deleteCategory(name){
  if([...ecarHmsParts,...ecarGobParts,...ecarWsParts].some(i=>i.cat===name)){ecar_toast(`"${name}" is in use`,4000);return;}
  if(!confirm(`Remove "${name}"?`))return;
  ecarCategories=ecarCategories.filter(c=>c!==name);
  ecar_renderCatList();ecar_populateCatDropdowns();
}

/* ═══════════════════════════════════
   SETUP
════════════════════════════════════ */

/* ── SUPPLIERS ── */
function ecar_renderSupList(){
  document.getElementById('ecar-sup-list').innerHTML=ecarSuppliers.sort().map(s=>
    `<span class="sup-pill">${ecar_esc(s)}<span class="sup-del" onclick="ecar_deleteSup('${ecar_esc(s)}')" title="Remove">×</span></span>`
  ).join('');
}
function ecar_addSupplier(){
  const inp=document.getElementById('ecar-new-sup');
  const name=inp.value.trim();
  if(!name)return;
  if(ecarSuppliers.includes(name)){ecar_toast('Supplier already exists');return;}
  ecarSuppliers.push(name);ecarSuppliers.sort();inp.value='';
  ecar_renderSupList();ecar_populateSupDropdowns();ecar_toast('"'+name+'" added');
}
function ecar_deleteSup(name){
  const inUse=[...ecarHmsParts,...ecarGobParts,...ecarWsParts].some(i=>i.supplier===name);
  if(inUse){ecar_toast('"'+name+'" is used by existing parts — reassign first',4000);return;}
  if(!confirm('Remove supplier "'+name+'"?'))return;
  ecarSuppliers=ecarSuppliers.filter(s=>s!==name);
  ecar_renderSupList();ecar_populateSupDropdowns();
}
function ecar_populateSupDropdowns(){
  const opts='<option value="">— Select supplier —</option>'+ecarSuppliers.sort().map(s=>`<option value="${ecar_esc(s)}">${ecar_esc(s)}</option>`).join('');
  document.querySelectorAll('#ecar-module .sup-select').forEach(el=>{
    const prev=el.value;
    el.innerHTML=opts;
    if(prev)el.value=prev;
  });
}

function ecar_renderSetup(){
  ecar_renderCatList();ecar_renderSupList();ecar_populateCatDropdowns();ecar_populateSupDropdowns();
  ecar_renderHmsList();ecar_renderGobList();ecar_renderWsList();
}
function ecar_setupTableRow(item,isGob,isWs){
  const inLocs=item.qtys.reduce((a,b)=>a+b,0);
  const prefix=isGob?'gp':isWs?'wp':'hp';
  const setFn=isGob?'gobSetField':isWs?'wsSetField':'hmsSetField';
  const resetFn=isGob?'resetGobQty':isWs?'resetWsQty':'resetHmsQty';
  const delFn=isGob?'deleteGobPart':isWs?'deleteWsPart':'deleteHmsPart';
  const resetLabel=isGob?'Both cars':isWs?'All 5':'All 6 pits';
  return`<tr>
    <td><input class="inline-input" value="${ecar_esc(item.name)}" style="width:100%;" onchange="ecar_${setFn}(${item.id},'name',this.value)"/></td>
    <td><input class="inline-input" value="${ecar_esc(item.sku)}" style="width:100%;font-family:monospace;font-size:11px;" onchange="${setFn}(${item.id},'sku',this.value)"/></td>
    <td><select class="inline-input" style="width:100%;padding:3px 4px;" onchange="ecar_${setFn}(${item.id},'cat',this.value)">
      ${ecarCategories.map(c=>`<option${c===item.cat?' selected':''}>${ecar_esc(c)}</option>`).join('')}
    </select></td>
    <td><input class="inline-input" type="number" min="0" value="${item.reqQty}" style="width:46px;" onchange="ecar_${setFn}(${item.id},'reqQty',this.value)"/></td>
    <td><div style="display:flex;align-items:center;gap:4px;">
      <input class="inline-input" type="number" min="0" id="r${prefix}-${item.id}" placeholder="qty" style="width:42px;"/>
      <button class="btn btn-sm" onclick="ecar_${resetFn}(${item.id})" style="font-size:10px;white-space:nowrap;">${resetLabel}</button>
    </div></td>
    <td><input class="inline-input" type="number" min="0" value="${item.srQty}" style="width:50px;" onchange="ecar_${setFn}(${item.id},'srQty',this.value)"/></td>
    <td><input class="inline-input" type="number" min="0" value="${item.srMin}" style="width:50px;" onchange="ecar_${setFn}(${item.id},'srMin',this.value)"/></td>
    <td style="text-align:center;color:#666;font-size:12px;">${inLocs}</td>
    <td><input class="inline-input" type="number" min="0" value="${item.trQty}" style="width:50px;" onchange="ecar_${setFn}(${item.id},'trQty',this.value)"/></td>
    <td><button class="del-btn" onclick="ecar_${delFn}(${item.id})">Remove</button></td>
  </tr>`;
}
function ecar_renderHmsList(){
  const s=(document.getElementById('ecar-hp-srch').value||'').toLowerCase();
  const fc=document.getElementById('ecar-hp-fcat').value||'';
  const items=ecarHmsParts.filter(i=>{
    if(s&&!i.name.toLowerCase().includes(s)&&!i.sku.toLowerCase().includes(s))return false;
    if(fc&&i.cat!==fc)return false;
    return true;
  });
  document.getElementById('ecar-hms-count').textContent=`${items.length} of ${ecarHmsParts.length}`;
  const tb=document.getElementById('ecar-hp-tbody');
  if(!items.length){tb.innerHTML='<tr><td colspan="10" style="text-align:center;padding:1.5rem;color:#888">No parts found</td></tr>';return;}
  tb.innerHTML=items.map(i=>ecar_setupTableRow(i,false,false)).join('');
}
function ecar_renderGobList(){
  const s=(document.getElementById('ecar-gp-srch').value||'').toLowerCase();
  const fc=document.getElementById('ecar-gp-fcat').value||'';
  const items=ecarGobParts.filter(i=>{
    if(s&&!i.name.toLowerCase().includes(s)&&!i.sku.toLowerCase().includes(s))return false;
    if(fc&&i.cat!==fc)return false;
    return true;
  });
  document.getElementById('ecar-gob-count').textContent=`${items.length} of ${ecarGobParts.length}`;
  const tb=document.getElementById('ecar-gp-tbody');
  if(!items.length){tb.innerHTML='<tr><td colspan="10" style="text-align:center;padding:1.5rem;color:#888">No parts found</td></tr>';return;}
  tb.innerHTML=items.map(i=>ecar_setupTableRow(i,true,false)).join('');
}
function ecar_renderWsList(){
  const s=(document.getElementById('ecar-wp-srch').value||'').toLowerCase();
  const fc=document.getElementById('ecar-wp-fcat').value||'';
  const items=ecarWsParts.filter(i=>{
    if(s&&!i.name.toLowerCase().includes(s)&&!i.sku.toLowerCase().includes(s))return false;
    if(fc&&i.cat!==fc)return false;
    return true;
  });
  document.getElementById('ecar-ws-count').textContent=`${items.length} of ${ecarWsParts.length}`;
  const tb=document.getElementById('ecar-wp-tbody');
  if(!items.length){tb.innerHTML='<tr><td colspan="10" style="text-align:center;padding:1.5rem;color:#888">No items found</td></tr>';return;}
  tb.innerHTML=items.map(i=>ecar_setupTableRow(i,false,true)).join('');
}

function ecar_hmsSetField(id,f,v){ecar_fieldSet(ecarHmsParts,id,f,v);}
function ecar_gobSetField(id,f,v){ecar_fieldSet(ecarGobParts,id,f,v);}
function ecar_wsSetField(id,f,v){ecar_fieldSet(ecarWsParts,id,f,v);}
function ecar_fieldSet(arr,id,f,v){
  const it=arr.find(x=>x.id===id);if(!it)return;
  if(f==='name')it.name=v.trim()||it.name;
  else if(f==='sku')it.sku=v.trim();
  else if(f==='cat')it.cat=v;
  else if(f==='reqQty')it.reqQty=Math.max(0,parseInt(v)||0);
  else if(f==='srQty'){it.srQty=Math.max(0,parseInt(v)||0);ecar_syncSrAcrossCatalogs(it.sku,it.srQty);}
  else if(f==='srMin'){it.srMin=Math.max(0,parseInt(v)||0);ecar_syncSrMinAcrossCatalogs(it.sku,it.srMin);}
  else if(f==='trQty'){it.trQty=Math.max(0,parseInt(v)||0);ecar_syncTrAcrossCatalogs(it.sku,it.trQty);}
  else if(f==='srUsedGood'){it.srUsedGood=Math.max(0,parseInt(v)||0);ecar_syncSrUsedGoodAcross(it.sku,it.srUsedGood);}
  else if(f==='srUsedRepair'){it.srUsedRepair=Math.max(0,parseInt(v)||0);ecar_syncSrUsedRepairAcross(it.sku,it.srUsedRepair);}
  else if(f==='trUsedGood'){it.trUsedGood=Math.max(0,parseInt(v)||0);ecar_syncTrUsedGoodAcross(it.sku,it.trUsedGood);}
  else if(f==='trUsedRepair'){it.trUsedRepair=Math.max(0,parseInt(v)||0);ecar_syncTrUsedRepairAcross(it.sku,it.trUsedRepair);}
  else if(f==='wsUsedGood')it.wsUsedGood=Math.max(0,parseInt(v)||0);
  else if(f==='wsUsedRepair')it.wsUsedRepair=Math.max(0,parseInt(v)||0);
  else if(f==='supplier')it.supplier=v;
  else if(f==='supplierPart')it.supplierPart=v.trim();
  else if(f==='unitCost')it.unitCost=Math.max(0,parseFloat(v)||0);
  else if(f==='lastOrderDate')it.lastOrderDate=v;
  else if(f==='lastOrderPrice')it.lastOrderPrice=Math.max(0,parseFloat(v)||0);
  ecar_renderAllViews();
  if(ecarHmsParts.includes(it))persistEcarHmsPart(it);
  else if(ecarGobParts.includes(it))persistEcarGobPart(it);
  else if(ecarWsParts.includes(it))persistEcarWsPart(it);
}

function ecar_resetHmsQty(id){
  const it=ecarHmsParts.find(x=>x.id===id);if(!it)return;
  const v=parseInt(document.getElementById('rhp-'+id)?.value);
  if(isNaN(v)||v<0){ecar_toast('Enter a valid quantity');return;}
  it.qtys=[v,v,v,v,v,v];
  document.getElementById('rhp-'+id).value='';
  ecar_renderAllViews();ecar_renderHmsList();
  ecar_toast(`All 6 HS/MS pits set to ${v} for "${it.name}"`);
}
function ecar_resetGobQty(id){
  const it=ecarGobParts.find(x=>x.id===id);if(!it)return;
  const v=parseInt(document.getElementById('rgp-'+id)?.value);
  if(isNaN(v)||v<0){ecar_toast('Enter a valid quantity');return;}
  it.qtys=[v,v];
  document.getElementById('rgp-'+id).value='';
  ecar_renderAllViews();ecar_renderGobList();
  ecar_toast(`Both Goblin pits set to ${v} for "${it.name}"`);
}
function ecar_resetWsQty(id){
  const it=ecarWsParts.find(x=>x.id===id);if(!it)return;
  const v=parseInt(document.getElementById('rwp-'+id)?.value);
  if(isNaN(v)||v<0){ecar_toast('Enter a valid quantity');return;}
  it.qtys=[v,v,v,v,v];
  document.getElementById('rwp-'+id).value='';
  ecar_renderAllViews();ecar_renderWsList();
  ecar_toast(`All workspaces set to ${v} for "${it.name}"`);
}

function ecar_addHmsPart(){
  const name=document.getElementById('ecar-hf-name').value.trim();
  if(!name){ecar_toast('Enter a part name');return;}
  const q=parseInt(document.getElementById('ecar-hf-cqty').value)||0;
  ecarHmsParts.push({id:ecarNextHmsId++,name,sku:document.getElementById('ecar-hf-sku').value.trim(),
    cat:document.getElementById('ecar-hf-cat').value,reqQty:parseInt(document.getElementById('ecar-hf-req').value)||1,
    qtys:[q,q,q,q,q,q],srQty:parseInt(document.getElementById('ecar-hf-srqty').value)||0,
    srMin:parseInt(document.getElementById('ecar-hf-srmin').value)||1,trQty:0,
    supplier:document.getElementById('ecar-hf-sup').value,supplierPart:document.getElementById('ecar-hf-suppart').value.trim(),
    unitCost:parseFloat(document.getElementById('ecar-hf-cost').value)||0,lastOrderDate:'',lastOrderPrice:0});
  ['hf-name','hf-sku'].forEach(id=>document.getElementById(id).value='');
  document.getElementById('ecar-hf-req').value=1;document.getElementById('ecar-hf-cqty').value=0;
  document.getElementById('ecar-hf-srqty').value=0;document.getElementById('ecar-hf-srmin').value=1;
  ecar_renderSetup();ecar_renderAllViews();ecar_toast(`"${name}" added to HS/MS catalog`);
}
function ecar_addGoblinPart(){
  const name=document.getElementById('ecar-gf-name').value.trim();
  if(!name){ecar_toast('Enter a part name');return;}
  const q=parseInt(document.getElementById('ecar-gf-cqty').value)||0;
  ecarGobParts.push({id:ecarNextGobId++,name,sku:document.getElementById('ecar-gf-sku').value.trim(),
    cat:document.getElementById('ecar-gf-cat').value,reqQty:parseInt(document.getElementById('ecar-gf-req').value)||1,
    qtys:[q,q],srQty:parseInt(document.getElementById('ecar-gf-srqty').value)||0,
    srMin:parseInt(document.getElementById('ecar-gf-srmin').value)||1,trQty:0,
    supplier:document.getElementById('ecar-gf-sup').value,supplierPart:document.getElementById('ecar-gf-suppart').value.trim(),
    unitCost:parseFloat(document.getElementById('ecar-gf-cost').value)||0,lastOrderDate:'',lastOrderPrice:0});
  ['gf-name','gf-sku'].forEach(id=>document.getElementById(id).value='');
  document.getElementById('ecar-gf-req').value=1;document.getElementById('ecar-gf-cqty').value=0;
  document.getElementById('ecar-gf-srqty').value=0;document.getElementById('ecar-gf-srmin').value=1;
  ecar_renderSetup();ecar_renderAllViews();ecar_toast(`"${name}" added to Goblin catalog`);
}
function ecar_addWsPart(){
  const name=document.getElementById('ecar-wf-name').value.trim();
  if(!name){ecar_toast('Enter an item name');return;}
  const q=parseInt(document.getElementById('ecar-wf-wqty').value)||0;
  ecarWsParts.push({id:ecarNextWsId++,name,sku:document.getElementById('ecar-wf-sku').value.trim(),
    cat:document.getElementById('ecar-wf-cat').value,reqQty:parseInt(document.getElementById('ecar-wf-req').value)||1,
    qtys:[q,q,q,q,q],srQty:parseInt(document.getElementById('ecar-wf-srqty').value)||0,
    srMin:parseInt(document.getElementById('ecar-wf-srmin').value)||1,trQty:0,
    supplier:document.getElementById('ecar-wf-sup').value,supplierPart:document.getElementById('ecar-wf-suppart').value.trim(),
    unitCost:parseFloat(document.getElementById('ecar-wf-cost').value)||0,lastOrderDate:'',lastOrderPrice:0});
  ['wf-name','wf-sku'].forEach(id=>document.getElementById(id).value='');
  document.getElementById('ecar-wf-req').value=1;document.getElementById('ecar-wf-wqty').value=0;
  document.getElementById('ecar-wf-srqty').value=0;document.getElementById('ecar-wf-srmin').value=1;
  ecar_renderSetup();ecar_renderAllViews();ecar_toast(`"${name}" added to workspace catalog`);
}
function ecar_deleteHmsPart(id){ecar_deletePart(ecarHmsParts,'hms',id);}
function ecar_deleteGobPart(id){ecar_deletePart(ecarGobParts,'gob',id);}
function ecar_deleteWsPart(id){ecar_deletePart(ecarWsParts,'ws',id);}
function ecar_deletePart(arr,type,id){
  const it=arr.find(x=>x.id===id);if(!it)return;
  if(!confirm(`Remove "${it.name}"?\n\nThis cannot be undone.`))return;
  if(type==='hms'){deleteEcarHmsPart(id);ecarHmsParts=ecarHmsParts.filter(x=>x.id!==id);}
  else if(type==='gob'){deleteEcarGobPart(id);ecarGobParts=ecarGobParts.filter(x=>x.id!==id);}
  else{deleteEcarWsPart(id);ecarWsParts=ecarWsParts.filter(x=>x.id!==id);}
  ecar_renderSetup();ecar_renderAllViews();ecar_toast(`"${it.name}" removed`);
}

/* ═══════════════════════════════════
   CARS PAGE
════════════════════════════════════ */
function ecar_renderCars(){
  const s=document.getElementById('ecar-cars-srch').value.toLowerCase();
  const fc=document.getElementById('ecar-cars-fcat').value;
  const fs=document.getElementById('ecar-cars-fstk').value;
  const hint=document.getElementById('ecar-cars-hint');
  const thead=document.getElementById('ecar-cars-thead');
  const tb=document.getElementById('ecar-cars-tbody');

  /* Group tabs */
  let gth=`<div class="tab ${ecarActiveGroup==='all'?'active':''}" onclick="ecar_setGroup('all')">All pits</div>`;
  GROUPS.forEach(g=>{
    const parts=ecar_partsForGroup(g.id);
    const idxs=ecar_carIndicesForGroup(g.id);
    let low=0,out=0;
    parts.forEach(p=>idxs.forEach(i=>{const st=ecar_qStatus(p.qtys[i],p.reqQty);if(st==='out')out++;else if(st==='low')low++;}));
    const hasOut=out>0,hasLow=low>0;
    gth+=`<div class="tab ${ecarActiveGroup===g.id?'active':''}" onclick="ecar_setGroup('${g.id}')">
      <span class="car-dot" style="background:${g.color}"></span>${g.name}
      ${hasOut?`<span class="badge bd">${out}</span>`:hasLow?`<span class="badge bw">${low}</span>`:''}
    </div>`;
  });
  document.getElementById('ecar-cars-group-tabs').innerHTML=gth;

  /* Car tabs (shown when a group is selected) */
  const carTabsEl=document.getElementById('ecar-cars-car-tabs');
  if(ecarActiveGroup==='all'){
    carTabsEl.innerHTML='';
  } else {
    const g=GROUPS.find(x=>x.id===ecarActiveGroup);
    const parts=ecar_partsForGroup(g.id);
    const idxs=ecar_carIndicesForGroup(g.id);
    let cth=`<div class="group-tab ${ecarActiveCar==='all'?'active':''}" onclick="ecar_setCar('all')">All ${g.name}</div>`;
    g.cars.forEach((car,ci)=>{
      const idx=idxs[ci];
      const out=parts.filter(p=>ecar_qStatus(p.qtys[idx],p.reqQty)==='out').length;
      const low=parts.filter(p=>ecar_qStatus(p.qtys[idx],p.reqQty)==='low').length;
      cth+=`<div class="group-tab ${ecarActiveCar===car?'active':''}" onclick="ecar_setCar('${car}')">
        <span class="car-dot" style="background:${g.color}"></span>Car ${car}
        ${out>0?`<span class="badge bd">${out}</span>`:low>0?`<span class="badge bw">${low}</span>`:''}
      </div>`;
    });
    carTabsEl.innerHTML=cth;
  }

  /* Determine what to render */
  const isSingleCar=ecarActiveGroup!=='all'&&ecarActiveCar!=='all';
  const isGroupOverview=ecarActiveGroup!=='all'&&ecarActiveCar==='all';
  const isAllOverview=ecarActiveGroup==='all';

  if(isAllOverview||isGroupOverview){
    /* Overview — read only, show per-pit qty columns for the visible pits */
    const displayGroups=ecarActiveGroup==='all'?GROUPS:[GROUPS.find(x=>x.id===ecarActiveGroup)];
    hint.innerHTML=`<span><strong>Overview — read only.</strong> Select a group then a car to take inventory or top up.</span>`;
    hint.style.cssText='font-size:11px;color:#888;margin-bottom:.625rem;padding:7px 11px;background:#f9f9f7;border-radius:7px;border:1px solid #e5e5e3;display:flex;align-items:center;justify-content:space-between;gap:10px;flex-wrap:wrap;';

    if(ecarActiveGroup==='all'){
      /* All pits — show group summary */
      thead.innerHTML=`<tr>
        <th style="width:20%">Part name</th>
        <th style="width:9%">Bin #</th>
        <th style="width:9%">Category</th>
        <th style="width:12%"><span style="display:inline-flex;align-items:center;gap:3px"><span class="car-dot" style="background:#185FA5"></span>HS total|MS total|Goblin total</span></th>
        <th style="width:12%"><span style="display:inline-flex;align-items:center;gap:3px"><span class="car-dot" style="background:#0F9D58"></span>HS total|MS total|Goblin total</span></th>
        <th style="width:12%"><span style="display:inline-flex;align-items:center;gap:3px"><span class="car-dot" style="background:#BA7517"></span>HS total|MS total|Goblin total</span></th>
        <th style="width:13%">Have / Need</th>
        <th style="width:13%">Shortfall</th>
      </tr>`;
      /* Combine all parts by SKU for unified overview */
      const allBySkuMap=new Map();
      [...ecarHmsParts,...ecarGobParts].forEach(p=>{
        if(!allBySkuMap.has(p.sku)){
          allBySkuMap.set(p.sku,{name:p.name,sku:p.sku,cat:p.cat,reqQty:p.reqQty,
            hsTotal:0,msTotal:0,gobTotal:0,hsReq:0,msReq:0,gobReq:0});
        }
        const ex=allBySkuMap.get(p.sku);
        const isHms=ecarHmsParts.includes(p);
        if(isHms){
          ex.hsTotal+=p.qtys[0]+p.qtys[1]+p.qtys[2];
          ex.msTotal+=p.qtys[3]+p.qtys[4]+p.qtys[5];
          ex.hsReq+=p.reqQty*3;ex.msReq+=p.reqQty*3;
        } else {
          ex.gobTotal+=p.qtys[0]+p.qtys[1];
          ex.gobReq+=p.reqQty*2;
        }
      });
      const allItems=Array.from(allBySkuMap.values()).filter(i=>{
        if(fc&&i.cat!==fc)return false;
        if(s&&!i.name.toLowerCase().includes(s)&&!i.sku.toLowerCase().includes(s))return false;
        return true;
      });
      if(!allItems.length){tb.innerHTML='<tr><td colspan="8" style="text-align:center;padding:2rem;color:#888">No parts found</td></tr>';return;}
      tb.innerHTML=allItems.map(item=>{
        const totalHave=item.hsTotal+item.msTotal+item.gobTotal;
        const totalReq=item.hsReq+item.msReq+item.gobReq;
        const totalShort=Math.max(0,totalReq-totalHave);
        const fullyStocked=totalShort===0;
        const hsShort=Math.max(0,item.hsReq-item.hsTotal);
        const msShort=Math.max(0,item.msReq-item.msTotal);
        const gobShort=Math.max(0,item.gobReq-item.gobTotal);
        const sfParts=[];
        if(hsShort>0)sfParts.push(`<span style="display:inline-flex;align-items:center;gap:2px;font-size:11px;color:#721c24;font-weight:600;margin-right:4px"><span class="car-dot" style="background:#185FA5"></span>HS −${hsShort}</span>`);
        if(msShort>0)sfParts.push(`<span style="display:inline-flex;align-items:center;gap:2px;font-size:11px;color:#721c24;font-weight:600;margin-right:4px"><span class="car-dot" style="background:#0F9D58"></span>MS −${msShort}</span>`);
        if(gobShort>0)sfParts.push(`<span style="display:inline-flex;align-items:center;gap:2px;font-size:11px;color:#721c24;font-weight:600;margin-right:4px"><span class="car-dot" style="background:#BA7517"></span>Gob −${gobShort}</span>`);
        const wsStatus=fullyStocked?'ok':totalHave===0?'out':'low';
        const hsSt=item.hsReq>0?(item.hsTotal===0?'out':item.hsTotal<item.hsReq?'low':'ok'):'ok';
        const msSt=item.msReq>0?(item.msTotal===0?'out':item.msTotal<item.msReq?'low':'ok'):'ok';
        const gobSt=item.gobReq>0?(item.gobTotal===0?'out':item.gobTotal<item.gobReq?'low':'ok'):'ok';
        return`<tr class="${wsStatus==='out'?'row-out':wsStatus==='low'?'row-low':''}">
          <td style="font-weight:500" title="${ecar_esc(item.name)}">${item.name}</td>
          <td style="font-family:monospace;font-size:10px;color:#888">${item.sku}</td>
          <td style="color:#888;font-size:11px">${item.cat}</td>
          <td style="text-align:center;font-weight:500;${hsSt==='out'?'color:#721c24':hsSt==='low'?'color:#856404':''}">${item.hsTotal}</td>
          <td style="text-align:center;font-weight:500;${msSt==='out'?'color:#721c24':msSt==='low'?'color:#856404':''}">${item.msTotal}</td>
          <td style="text-align:center;font-weight:500;${gobSt==='out'?'color:#721c24':gobSt==='low'?'color:#856404':''}">${item.gobReq>0?item.gobTotal:'—'}</td>
          <td style="white-space:nowrap"><span style="font-weight:500">${totalHave}</span>${totalShort>0?` <span style="color:#721c24;font-weight:600;font-size:12px">/ −${totalShort}</span>`:`<span style="color:#aaa;font-size:10px"> / full</span>`}</td>
          <td style="white-space:nowrap">${fullyStocked?`<span style="color:#155724;font-size:11px">✓ All stocked</span>`:sfParts.join('')}</td>
        </tr>`;
      }).join('');
    } else {
      /* Group overview — show individual pits in this group */
      const g=GROUPS.find(x=>x.id===ecarActiveGroup);
      const parts=ecar_partsForGroup(g.id);
      const idxs=ecar_carIndicesForGroup(g.id);
      const carCols=g.cars.map((car,ci)=>`<th style="width:${Math.floor(40/g.cars.length)}%"><span style="display:inline-flex;align-items:center;gap:3px"><span class="car-dot" style="background:${g.color}"></span>Car ${car}</span></th>`).join('');
      thead.innerHTML=`<tr>
        <th style="width:20%">Part name</th>
        <th style="width:10%">Bin #</th>
        <th style="width:10%">Category</th>
        ${carCols}
        <th style="width:10%">Req/pit</th>
        <th style="width:13%">Shortfall</th>
      </tr>`;
      const filtered=parts.filter(i=>{
        if(fc&&i.cat!==fc)return false;
        if(s&&!i.name.toLowerCase().includes(s)&&!i.sku.toLowerCase().includes(s))return false;
        return true;
      });
      if(!filtered.length){tb.innerHTML=`<tr><td colspan="${4+g.cars.length}" style="text-align:center;padding:2rem;color:#888">No parts found</td></tr>`;return;}
      tb.innerHTML=filtered.map(item=>{
        const ws=ecar_worstOf(idxs.map(i=>ecar_qStatus(item.qtys[i],item.reqQty)));
        const qCells=idxs.map(i=>{
          const st=ecar_qStatus(item.qtys[i],item.reqQty);
          const c=st==='out'?'color:#721c24':st==='low'?'color:#856404':'color:#1a1a1a';
          return`<td style="text-align:center;font-size:13px;font-weight:500;${c}">${item.qtys[i]}</td>`;
        }).join('');
        const shorts=idxs.map((i,ci)=>({short:Math.max(0,item.reqQty-item.qtys[i]),car:g.cars[ci]})).filter(x=>x.short>0);
        const sfCell=shorts.length===0?`<span style="color:#155724;font-size:11px">✓ All stocked</span>`:
          shorts.map(x=>`<span style="display:inline-flex;align-items:center;gap:2px;margin-right:4px;font-size:11px;color:#721c24;font-weight:600"><span class="car-dot" style="background:${g.color}"></span>${x.car} −${x.short}</span>`).join('');
        return`<tr class="${ws==='out'?'row-out':ws==='low'?'row-low':''}">
          <td style="font-weight:500" title="${ecar_esc(item.name)}">${item.name}</td>
          <td style="font-family:monospace;font-size:10px;color:#888">${item.sku}</td>
          <td style="color:#888;font-size:11px">${item.cat}</td>
          ${qCells}
          <td style="text-align:center;color:#666;font-weight:500">${item.reqQty}</td>
          <td>${sfCell}</td>
        </tr>`;
      }).join('');
    }
  } else {
    /* Single car — inventory taking */
    const g=GROUPS.find(x=>x.id===ecarActiveGroup);
    const carIdx=ecar_carIndicesForGroup(g.id)[g.cars.indexOf(ecarActiveCar)];
    const parts=ecar_partsForGroup(g.id);
    hint.innerHTML=`
      <span><strong style="color:${g.color}">Pit ${ecarActiveCar} — taking inventory.</strong> Use + / − to count what's physically in this pit.</span>
      <button class="btn btn-sm" style="background:${g.color};color:#fff;border-color:${g.color};white-space:nowrap;" onclick="ecar_openCarTopup('${g.id}','${ecarActiveCar}',${carIdx})">
        <svg width="11" height="11" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2.5"><polyline points="17 11 12 6 7 11"/><line x1="12" y1="18" x2="12" y2="6"/></svg>
        Top up Pit ${ecarActiveCar}
      </button>`;
    hint.style.cssText=`font-size:11px;color:#888;margin-bottom:.625rem;padding:7px 11px;background:${g.light};border-radius:7px;border:1px solid ${g.color}44;display:flex;align-items:center;justify-content:space-between;gap:10px;flex-wrap:wrap;`;
    thead.innerHTML=`<tr>
      <th style="width:33%">Part name</th>
      <th style="width:13%">Bin #</th>
      <th style="width:14%">Category</th>
      <th style="width:20%">Qty — Pit <span style="color:${g.color};font-weight:600">${ecarActiveCar}</span></th>
      <th style="width:11%">Required</th>
      <th style="width:9%">Status</th>
    </tr>`;
    const filtered=parts.filter(i=>{
      const st=ecar_qStatus(i.qtys[carIdx],i.reqQty);
      if(fs==='ok'&&st!=='ok')return false;
      if(fs==='low'&&st!=='low')return false;
      if(fc&&i.cat!==fc)return false;
      if(s&&!i.name.toLowerCase().includes(s)&&!i.sku.toLowerCase().includes(s))return false;
      return true;
    });
    if(!filtered.length){tb.innerHTML='<tr><td colspan="6" style="text-align:center;padding:2rem;color:#888">No parts found</td></tr>';return;}
    tb.innerHTML=filtered.map(item=>{
      const q=item.qtys[carIdx];
      const st=ecar_qStatus(q,item.reqQty);
      const qc=st==='out'?'color:#721c24':st==='low'?'color:#856404':'';
      return`<tr class="${st==='out'?'row-out':st==='low'?'row-low':''}">
        <td style="font-weight:500" title="${ecar_esc(item.name)}">${item.name}</td>
        <td style="font-family:monospace;font-size:10px;color:#888">${item.sku}</td>
        <td style="color:#888;font-size:11px">${item.cat}</td>
        <td><div class="qty-ctrl">
          <button class="qb" onclick="ecar_carChgQty('${g.id}',${item.id},${carIdx},-1)">−</button>
          <span class="qn" style="${qc}">${q}</span>
          <button class="qb" onclick="ecar_carChgQty('${g.id}',${item.id},${carIdx},1)">+</button>
        </div></td>
        <td style="color:#666">${item.reqQty}</td>
        <td>${ecar_badge(st)}</td>
      </tr>`;
    }).join('');
  }
}

function ecar_setGroup(g){
  ecarActiveGroup=g;
  if(g==='all'){ecarActiveCar='all';}
  else{ecarActiveCar='all';}
  ecar_renderCars();
}
function ecar_setCar(car){ecarActiveCar=car;ecar_renderCars();}
function ecar_carChgQty(gid,id,carIdx,d){
  const arr=ecar_partsForGroup(gid);
  const it=arr.find(x=>x.id===id);
  if(it){it.qtys[carIdx]=Math.max(0,it.qtys[carIdx]+d);ecar_renderCars();
    if(gid==='hs'||gid==='ms')persistEcarHmsPart(it);
    else if(gid==='gob')persistEcarGobPart(it);}
}

/* ═══════════════════════════════════
   WORKSPACES PAGE
════════════════════════════════════ */
function ecar_renderWorkspaces(){
  const s=document.getElementById('ecar-ws-srch').value.toLowerCase();
  const fc=document.getElementById('ecar-ws-fcat').value;
  const fs=document.getElementById('ecar-ws-fstk').value;
  const hint=document.getElementById('ecar-ws-hint');
  const thead=document.getElementById('ecar-ws-thead');
  const tb=document.getElementById('ecar-ws-tbody');

  let th=`<div class="tab ${ecarActiveWs==='all'?'active':''}" onclick="ecar_setWs('all')">All workspaces</div>`;
  WORKSPACES.forEach((w,i)=>{
    const out=ecarWsParts.filter(x=>ecar_qStatus(x.qtys[i],x.reqQty)==='out').length;
    const low=ecarWsParts.filter(x=>ecar_qStatus(x.qtys[i],x.reqQty)==='low').length;
    th+=`<div class="tab ${ecarActiveWs==i?'active':''}" onclick="ecar_setWs(${i})">
      <span class="team-dot" style="width:8px;height:8px;border-radius:50%;background:${w.color};flex-shrink:0;display:inline-block"></span>${w.name}
      ${out>0?`<span class="badge bd">${out}</span>`:low>0?`<span class="badge bw">${low}</span>`:''}
    </div>`;
  });
  document.getElementById('ecar-ws-tabs').innerHTML=th;

  if(ecarActiveWs==='all'){
    hint.innerHTML='<span><strong>All workspaces — overview.</strong> Select a workspace tab to take inventory or top up.</span>';
    hint.style.cssText='font-size:11px;color:#888;margin-bottom:.625rem;padding:7px 11px;background:#f9f9f7;border-radius:7px;border:1px solid #e5e5e3;display:flex;align-items:center;justify-content:space-between;gap:10px;flex-wrap:wrap;';
    const wsNames=WORKSPACES.map(w=>w.name);
    const wsCols=WORKSPACES.map((w,i)=>`<th style="width:8%"><span style="display:inline-flex;align-items:center;gap:2px;font-size:10px"><span style="width:6px;height:6px;border-radius:50%;background:${w.color};display:inline-block"></span>${w.name.replace('Tool Box ','TB')}</span></th>`).join('');
    thead.innerHTML=`<tr>
      <th style="width:18%">Item name</th>
      <th style="width:9%">Bin #</th>
      <th style="width:9%">Category</th>
      ${wsCols}
      <th style="width:7%">Req/ws</th>
      <th style="width:10%">Have / Need</th>
      <th style="width:11%">Shortfall</th>
    </tr>`;
    const filtered=ecarWsParts.filter(i=>{
      if(fc&&i.cat!==fc)return false;
      if(s&&!i.name.toLowerCase().includes(s)&&!i.sku.toLowerCase().includes(s))return false;
      return true;
    });
    if(!filtered.length){tb.innerHTML=`<tr><td colspan="${6+WORKSPACES.length}" style="text-align:center;padding:2rem;color:#888">No items found</td></tr>`;return;}
    tb.innerHTML=filtered.map(item=>{
      const totalHave=item.qtys.reduce((a,b)=>a+b,0);
      const req=item.reqQty;
      const totalShort=Math.max(0,req*WORKSPACES.length-totalHave);
      const fullyStocked=totalShort===0;
      const ws=ecar_worstOf(item.qtys.map(q=>ecar_qStatus(q,req)));
      const qCells=item.qtys.map((q,wi)=>{
        const st=ecar_qStatus(q,req);
        const c=st==='out'?'color:#721c24':st==='low'?'color:#856404':'color:#1a1a1a';
        return`<td style="text-align:center;font-size:12px;font-weight:500;${c}">${q}</td>`;
      }).join('');
      const shorts=item.qtys.map((q,wi)=>({short:Math.max(0,req-q),name:WORKSPACES[wi].name,color:WORKSPACES[wi].color})).filter(x=>x.short>0);
      const sfCell=fullyStocked?`<span style="color:#155724;font-size:11px">✓ All stocked</span>`:
        shorts.map(x=>`<span style="display:inline-flex;align-items:center;gap:2px;margin-right:3px;font-size:11px;color:#721c24;font-weight:600"><span style="width:6px;height:6px;border-radius:50%;background:${x.color};display:inline-block"></span>−${x.short}</span>`).join('');
      return`<tr class="${ws==='out'?'row-out':ws==='low'?'row-low':''}">
        <td style="font-weight:500" title="${ecar_esc(item.name)}">${item.name}</td>
        <td style="font-family:monospace;font-size:10px;color:#888">${item.sku}</td>
        <td style="color:#888;font-size:11px">${item.cat}</td>
        ${qCells}
        <td style="text-align:center;color:#666;font-weight:500">${req}</td>
        <td>${totalShort>0?`<span style="font-weight:500">${totalHave}</span> <span style="color:#721c24;font-weight:600;font-size:12px">/ −${totalShort}</span>`:`<span style="color:#155724;font-weight:600">${totalHave}</span> <span style="color:#aaa;font-size:10px">/ full</span>`}</td>
        <td>${sfCell}</td>
      </tr>`;
    }).join('');
  } else {
    const wi=+ecarActiveWs;
    const w=WORKSPACES[wi];
    hint.innerHTML=`
      <span><strong style="color:${w.color}">${w.name} — taking inventory.</strong> Use + / − to count what's physically here.</span>
      <button class="btn btn-sm" style="background:${w.color};color:#fff;border-color:${w.color};white-space:nowrap;" onclick="ecar_openWsTopup(${wi})">
        <svg width="11" height="11" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2.5"><polyline points="17 11 12 6 7 11"/><line x1="12" y1="18" x2="12" y2="6"/></svg>
        Top up ${w.name}
      </button>`;
    hint.style.cssText=`font-size:11px;color:#888;margin-bottom:.625rem;padding:7px 11px;background:${w.light};border-radius:7px;border:1px solid ${w.color}44;display:flex;align-items:center;justify-content:space-between;gap:10px;flex-wrap:wrap;`;
    thead.innerHTML=`<tr>
      <th style="width:33%">Item name</th>
      <th style="width:13%">Bin #</th>
      <th style="width:14%">Category</th>
      <th style="width:20%">Qty — <span style="color:${w.color};font-weight:600">${w.name}</span></th>
      <th style="width:11%">Required</th>
      <th style="width:9%">Status</th>
    </tr>`;
    const filtered=ecarWsParts.filter(i=>{
      const st=ecar_qStatus(i.qtys[wi],i.reqQty);
      if(fs==='ok'&&st!=='ok')return false;
      if(fs==='low'&&st!=='low')return false;
      if(fc&&i.cat!==fc)return false;
      if(s&&!i.name.toLowerCase().includes(s)&&!i.sku.toLowerCase().includes(s))return false;
      return true;
    });
    if(!filtered.length){tb.innerHTML='<tr><td colspan="6" style="text-align:center;padding:2rem;color:#888">No items found</td></tr>';return;}
    tb.innerHTML=filtered.map(item=>{
      const q=item.qtys[wi];
      const st=ecar_qStatus(q,item.reqQty);
      const qc=st==='out'?'color:#721c24':st==='low'?'color:#856404':'';
      return`<tr class="${st==='out'?'row-out':st==='low'?'row-low':''}">
        <td style="font-weight:500" title="${ecar_esc(item.name)}">${item.name}</td>
        <td style="font-family:monospace;font-size:10px;color:#888">${item.sku}</td>
        <td style="color:#888;font-size:11px">${item.cat}</td>
        <td><div class="qty-ctrl">
          <button class="qb" onclick="ecar_wsChgQty(${item.id},${wi},-1)">−</button>
          <span class="qn" style="${qc}">${q}</span>
          <button class="qb" onclick="ecar_wsChgQty(${item.id},${wi},1)">+</button>
        </div></td>
        <td style="color:#666">${item.reqQty}</td>
        <td>${ecar_badge(st)}</td>
      </tr>`;
    }).join('');
  }
}
function ecar_setWs(w){ecarActiveWs=w;ecar_renderWorkspaces();}
function ecar_wsChgQty(id,wi,d){
  const it=ecarWsParts.find(x=>x.id===id);
  if(it){it.qtys[wi]=Math.max(0,it.qtys[wi]+d);ecar_renderWorkspaces();}
}

/* ═══════════════════════════════════
   RACE TRAILER PAGE
════════════════════════════════════ */
function ecar_renderTrailer(){
  const s=document.getElementById('ecar-tr-srch').value.toLowerCase();
  const fc=document.getElementById('ecar-tr-fcat').value;
  const fs=document.getElementById('ecar-tr-fstk').value;
  /* Build unified trailer list — one row per unique SKU */
  const trMap=new Map();
  [...ecarHmsParts,...ecarGobParts,...ecarWsParts].forEach(item=>{
    if(!trMap.has(item.sku)){
      trMap.set(item.sku,{name:item.name,sku:item.sku,cat:item.cat,trQty:item.trQty,srQty:item.srQty,srMin:item.srMin,trMin:Math.max(2,item.srMin)});
    } else {
      const ex=trMap.get(item.sku);
      ex.trMin=Math.max(ex.trMin,Math.max(2,item.srMin));
    }
  });
  const allItems=Array.from(trMap.values());
  /* Check for items below trailer min */
  const belowMin=allItems.filter(i=>i.trQty<=i.trMin);
  if(belowMin.length>0){
    document.getElementById('ecar-trailer-hint').innerHTML=`
      <span><strong>Race Trailer.</strong> ${belowMin.length} item${belowMin.length>1?'s':''} below minimum — restock from Stock Room before next event.</span>
      <button class="btn btn-teal btn-sm" onclick="ecar_openTrailerRestock()">
        <svg width="11" height="11" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2.5"><polyline points="17 11 12 6 7 11"/><line x1="12" y1="18" x2="12" y2="6"/></svg>
        Restock from Stock Room
      </button>`;
    document.getElementById('ecar-trailer-hint').style.cssText='font-size:11px;color:#888;margin-bottom:.625rem;padding:7px 11px;background:#FDF4F1;border-radius:7px;border:1px solid #D85A3044;display:flex;align-items:center;justify-content:space-between;gap:10px;flex-wrap:wrap;';
  } else {
    document.getElementById('ecar-trailer-hint').innerHTML=`
      <span><strong>Race Trailer — all stocked.</strong> Verify quantities after each race. Use "Restock from Stock Room" when items drop below minimum.</span>
      <button class="btn btn-teal btn-sm" onclick="ecar_openTrailerRestock()">
        <svg width="11" height="11" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2.5"><polyline points="17 11 12 6 7 11"/><line x1="12" y1="18" x2="12" y2="6"/></svg>
        Restock from Stock Room
      </button>`;
    document.getElementById('ecar-trailer-hint').style.cssText='font-size:11px;color:#888;margin-bottom:.625rem;padding:7px 11px;background:#f9f9f7;border-radius:7px;border:1px solid #e5e5e3;display:flex;align-items:center;justify-content:space-between;gap:10px;flex-wrap:wrap;';
  }
  const filtered=allItems.filter(i=>{
    const st=ecar_trStatus(i.trQty,i.trMin);
    if(fs==='ok'&&st!=='ok')return false;
    if(fs==='low'&&st==='ok')return false;
    if(fc&&i.cat!==fc)return false;
    if(s&&!i.name.toLowerCase().includes(s)&&!i.sku.toLowerCase().includes(s))return false;
    return true;
  });
  const tb=document.getElementById('ecar-tr-tbody');
  if(!filtered.length){tb.innerHTML='<tr><td colspan="6" style="text-align:center;padding:2rem;color:#888">No items found</td></tr>';return;}
  tb.innerHTML=filtered.map(item=>{
    const st=ecar_trStatus(item.trQty,item.trMin);
    const qc=st==='out'?'color:#721c24':st==='low'?'color:#856404':'';
    const tug=item.trUsedGood||0; const tur=item.trUsedRepair||0;
    return`<tr class="${st==='out'?'row-out':st==='low'?'row-low':''}">
      <td style="font-weight:500" title="${ecar_esc(item.name)}">${item.name}</td>
      <td style="font-family:monospace;font-size:10px;color:#888">${item.sku}</td>
      <td style="color:#888;font-size:11px">${item.cat}</td>
      <td><div class="qty-ctrl">
        <button class="qb" onclick="ecar_trChgQty('${item.sku}','new',-1)">−</button>
        <span class="qn" style="${qc}">${item.trQty}</span>
        <button class="qb" onclick="ecar_trChgQty('${item.sku}','new',1)">+</button>
      </div></td>
      <td><div class="qty-ctrl">
        <button class="qb" onclick="ecar_trChgQty('${item.sku}','usedGood',-1)">−</button>
        <span class="qn" style="${tug>0?'color:#185FA5':''}">${tug}</span>
        <button class="qb" onclick="ecar_trChgQty('${item.sku}','usedGood',1)">+</button>
      </div></td>
      <td><div class="qty-ctrl">
        <button class="qb" onclick="ecar_trChgQty('${item.sku}','usedRepair',-1)">−</button>
        <span class="qn" style="${tur>0?'color:#856404':''}">${tur}</span>
        <button class="qb" onclick="ecar_trChgQty('${item.sku}','usedRepair',1)">+</button>
      </div></td>
      <td style="color:#666;text-align:center;">${item.trMin}</td>
      <td>${ecar_badge(st)}</td>
    </tr>`;
  }).join('');
}
function ecar_trChgQty(sku,field,d){
  const cur=[...ecarHmsParts,...ecarGobParts,...ecarWsParts].find(i=>i.sku===sku);
  if(!cur)return;
  if(field==='new')ecar_syncTrAcrossCatalogs(sku,Math.max(0,cur.trQty+d));
  else if(field==='usedGood')ecar_syncTrUsedGoodAcross(sku,Math.max(0,(cur.trUsedGood||0)+d));
  else if(field==='usedRepair')ecar_syncTrUsedRepairAcross(sku,Math.max(0,(cur.trUsedRepair||0)+d));
  ecar_renderTrailer();
  ecarHmsParts.filter(i=>i.sku===sku).forEach(persistEcarHmsPart);
  ecarGobParts.filter(i=>i.sku===sku).forEach(persistEcarGobPart);
  ecarWsParts.filter(i=>i.sku===sku).forEach(persistEcarWsPart);
}

/* ═══════════════════════════════════
   STOCK ROOM PAGE
════════════════════════════════════ */
function ecar_renderStockRoom(){
  const s=document.getElementById('ecar-sr-srch').value.toLowerCase();
  const fc=document.getElementById('ecar-sr-fcat').value;
  const fs=document.getElementById('ecar-sr-fstk').value;
  /* Build unique SKU list */
  const srMap=new Map();
  [...ecarHmsParts,...ecarGobParts,...ecarWsParts].forEach(item=>{
    if(!srMap.has(item.sku)){
      srMap.set(item.sku,{name:item.name,sku:item.sku,cat:item.cat,srQty:item.srQty,srMin:item.srMin});
    } else {
      const ex=srMap.get(item.sku);
      ex.srMin=Math.max(ex.srMin,item.srMin);
    }
  });
  const allItems=Array.from(srMap.values());
  const filtered=allItems.filter(i=>{
    const st=ecar_srStatus(i.srQty,i.srMin);
    if(fs==='ok'&&st!=='ok')return false;
    if(fs==='low'&&st==='ok')return false;
    if(fc&&i.cat!==fc)return false;
    if(s&&!i.name.toLowerCase().includes(s)&&!i.sku.toLowerCase().includes(s))return false;
    return true;
  });
  const tb=document.getElementById('ecar-sr-tbody');
  if(!filtered.length){tb.innerHTML='<tr><td colspan="6" style="text-align:center;padding:2rem;color:#888">No items found</td></tr>';return;}
  if(!filtered.length){tb.innerHTML='<tr><td colspan="8" style="text-align:center;padding:2rem;color:#888">No items found</td></tr>';return;}
  tb.innerHTML=filtered.map(item=>{
    const st=ecar_srStatus(item.srQty,item.srMin);
    const qc=st==='out'?'color:#721c24':st==='low'?'color:#856404':'';
    const ug=item.srUsedGood||0;const ur=item.srUsedRepair||0;
    return`<tr class="${st==='out'?'row-out':st==='low'?'row-low':''}">
      <td style="font-weight:500" title="${ecar_esc(item.name)}">${item.name}</td>
      <td style="font-family:monospace;font-size:10px;color:#888">${item.sku}</td>
      <td style="color:#888;font-size:11px">${item.cat}</td>
      <td><div class="qty-ctrl">
        <button class="qb" onclick="ecar_srChgQty('${item.sku}','new',-1)">−</button>
        <span class="qn" style="${qc}">${item.srQty}</span>
        <button class="qb" onclick="ecar_srChgQty('${item.sku}','new',1)">+</button>
      </div></td>
      <td><div class="qty-ctrl">
        <button class="qb" onclick="ecar_srChgQty('${item.sku}','usedGood',-1)">−</button>
        <span class="qn" style="${ug>0?'color:#185FA5':''}">${ug}</span>
        <button class="qb" onclick="ecar_srChgQty('${item.sku}','usedGood',1)">+</button>
      </div></td>
      <td><div class="qty-ctrl">
        <button class="qb" onclick="ecar_srChgQty('${item.sku}','usedRepair',-1)">−</button>
        <span class="qn" style="${ur>0?'color:#856404':''}">${ur}</span>
        <button class="qb" onclick="ecar_srChgQty('${item.sku}','usedRepair',1)">+</button>
      </div></td>
      <td style="color:#666;text-align:center;">${item.srMin}</td>
      <td>${ecar_badge(st)}</td>
    </tr>`;
  }).join('');
}
function ecar_srChgQty(sku,field,d){
  const cur=ecar_getSrQtyBySku(sku);
  ecar_syncSrAcrossCatalogs(sku,Math.max(0,cur.srQty+d));
  ecar_renderStockRoom();
}

/* ═══════════════════════════════════
   MASTER INVENTORY PAGE
════════════════════════════════════ */
function ecar_renderMaster(){
  const s=document.getElementById('ecar-master-srch').value.toLowerCase();
  const fc=document.getElementById('ecar-master-fcat').value;
  const fs=document.getElementById('ecar-master-fstk').value;
  const masterMap=new Map();
  [...ecarHmsParts,...ecarGobParts,...ecarWsParts].forEach(item=>{
    const inLoc=item.qtys.reduce((a,b)=>a+b,0);
    const isHms=ecarHmsParts.includes(item);
    const isGob=ecarGobParts.includes(item);
    const isWs=ecarWsParts.includes(item);
    const carReq=isHms?item.reqQty*6:isGob?item.reqQty*2:0;
    const wsReq=isWs?item.reqQty*5:0;
    if(!masterMap.has(item.sku)){
      masterMap.set(item.sku,{name:item.name,sku:item.sku,cat:item.cat,
        srQty:item.srQty,srMin:item.srMin,trQty:item.trQty,
        srUsedGood:item.srUsedGood||0,srUsedRepair:item.srUsedRepair||0,
        trUsedGood:item.trUsedGood||0,trUsedRepair:item.trUsedRepair||0,
        wsUsedGood:isWs?(item.wsUsedGood||0):0,
        inCars:isWs?0:inLoc,inWs:isWs?inLoc:0,
        carReq,wsReq});
    } else {
      const ex=masterMap.get(item.sku);
      if(isWs){ex.inWs+=inLoc;ex.wsUsedGood+=(item.wsUsedGood||0);}
      else ex.inCars+=inLoc;
      ex.carReq+=carReq;ex.wsReq+=wsReq;
      ex.srMin=Math.max(ex.srMin,item.srMin);
      ex.srUsedGood=Math.max(ex.srUsedGood,item.srUsedGood||0);
      ex.srUsedRepair=Math.max(ex.srUsedRepair,item.srUsedRepair||0);
      ex.trUsedGood=Math.max(ex.trUsedGood,item.trUsedGood||0);
    }
  });
  const allItems=Array.from(masterMap.values());
  const filtered=allItems.filter(i=>{
    const totalHave=i.srQty+i.trQty+i.inCars+i.inWs;
    const totalReq=i.carReq+i.wsReq;
    const sf=Math.max(0,totalReq-totalHave);
    if(fs==='low'&&sf===0)return false;
    if(fc&&i.cat!==fc)return false;
    if(s&&!i.name.toLowerCase().includes(s)&&!i.sku.toLowerCase().includes(s))return false;
    return true;
  });
  const tb=document.getElementById('ecar-master-tbody');
  if(!filtered.length){tb.innerHTML='<tr><td colspan="15" style="text-align:center;padding:2rem;color:#888">No items found</td></tr>';return;}
  tb.innerHTML=filtered.map(item=>{
    const srUG=item.srUsedGood||0,srUR=item.srUsedRepair||0;
    const trUG=item.trUsedGood||0;
    const wsUG=item.wsUsedGood||0;
    /* Available = new stock + used-good (serviceable) everywhere */
    const totalAvail=item.srQty+(item.trQty||0)+item.inCars+item.inWs+srUG+trUG+wsUG;
    const totalReq=item.carReq+item.wsReq;
    const sf=Math.max(0,totalReq-totalAvail);
    const srSt=ecar_srStatus(item.srQty,item.srMin);
    const overallSt=sf>0?(sf>=totalReq?'out':'low'):'ok';
    return`<tr class="${overallSt==='out'?'row-out':overallSt==='low'?'row-low':''}">
      <td style="font-weight:500" title="${ecar_esc(item.name)}">${item.name}</td>
      <td style="font-family:monospace;font-size:10px;color:#888">${item.sku}</td>
      <td style="color:#888;font-size:11px">${item.cat}</td>
      <td style="text-align:center;font-weight:500">${item.srQty}</td>
      <td style="text-align:center;color:#185FA5;font-weight:500">${srUG||'—'}</td>
      <td style="text-align:center;color:#856404;font-weight:500">${srUR||'—'}</td>
      <td style="text-align:center;font-weight:500">${item.trQty||0}</td>
      <td style="text-align:center;color:#185FA5">${trUG||'—'}</td>
      <td style="text-align:center;color:#666">${item.inCars}</td>
      <td style="text-align:center;color:#666">${item.inWs}</td>
      <td style="text-align:center;font-weight:600">${totalAvail}</td>
      <td style="text-align:center;color:#666">${totalReq||'—'}</td>
      <td style="text-align:center;font-weight:600;${sf>0?'color:#721c24':'color:#155724'}">${sf>0?'−'+sf:'✓'}</td>
      <td style="text-align:center;${srSt==='out'?'color:#721c24':srSt==='low'?'color:#856404':'color:#155724'}">${item.srMin}</td>
      <td>${ecar_badge(srSt)}</td>
    </tr>`;
  }).join('');
}

/* ═══════════════════════════════════
   TOP-UP MODAL
════════════════════════════════════ */
function ecar_openCarTopup(gid,carName,carIdx){
  ecarTopupCtx={type:'car',gid,carName,carIdx};
  ecarTopupSource='sr';
  document.getElementById('ecar-source-selector-wrap').style.display='block';
  document.getElementById('ecar-src-sr').classList.add('active');
  document.getElementById('ecar-src-tr').classList.remove('active');
  ecar_buildTopupModal(`Top up — Pit ${carName}`);
}
function ecar_openWsTopup(wi){
  ecarTopupCtx={type:'ws',wi};
  ecarTopupSource='sr';
  document.getElementById('ecar-source-selector-wrap').style.display='block';
  document.getElementById('ecar-src-sr').classList.add('active');
  document.getElementById('ecar-src-tr').classList.remove('active');
  ecar_buildTopupModal(`Top up — ${WORKSPACES[wi].name}`);
}
function ecar_openTrailerRestock(){
  ecarTopupCtx={type:'trailer'};
  ecarTopupSource='sr';
  document.getElementById('ecar-source-selector-wrap').style.display='none';
  ecar_buildTopupModal('Restock Race Trailer from Stock Room');
}
function ecar_setTopupSource(src){
  ecarTopupSource=src;
  document.getElementById('ecar-src-sr').classList.toggle('active',src==='sr');
  document.getElementById('ecar-src-tr').classList.toggle('active',src==='tr');
  ecar_buildTopupModal(document.getElementById('ecar-topup-title').textContent);
}
function ecar_buildTopupModal(title){
  document.getElementById('ecar-topup-title').textContent=title;
  const body=document.getElementById('ecar-topup-body');
  let shortItems=[];
  if(ecarTopupCtx.type==='car'){
    const parts=ecar_partsForGroup(ecarTopupCtx.gid);
    shortItems=parts.filter(i=>i.qtys[ecarTopupCtx.carIdx]<i.reqQty).map(i=>({
      id:i.id,name:i.name,sku:i.sku,
      has:i.qtys[ecarTopupCtx.carIdx],req:i.reqQty,
      avail:ecarTopupSource==='sr'?i.srQty:i.trQty,
      source:ecarTopupSource
    }));
  } else if(ecarTopupCtx.type==='ws'){
    shortItems=ecarWsParts.filter(i=>i.qtys[ecarTopupCtx.wi]<i.reqQty).map(i=>({
      id:i.id,name:i.name,sku:i.sku,
      has:i.qtys[ecarTopupCtx.wi],req:i.reqQty,
      avail:ecarTopupSource==='sr'?i.srQty:i.trQty,
      source:ecarTopupSource
    }));
  } else if(ecarTopupCtx.type==='trailer'){
    /* Restock trailer from SR — show items below trailer min */
    const trMap=new Map();
    [...ecarHmsParts,...ecarGobParts,...ecarWsParts].forEach(item=>{
      if(!trMap.has(item.sku)){
        const trMin=Math.max(2,item.srMin);
        trMap.set(item.sku,{id:item.id,name:item.name,sku:item.sku,
          has:item.trQty,req:trMin,avail:item.srQty,source:'sr'});
      }
    });
    shortItems=Array.from(trMap.values()).filter(i=>i.has<i.req);
  }
  if(!shortItems.length){
    body.innerHTML=`<div style="text-align:center;padding:2rem;color:#155724;font-weight:500;background:#E8F5E9;border-radius:8px;">
      <div style="font-size:24px;margin-bottom:.5rem">✓</div>
      Fully stocked — nothing to top up!
    </div>`;
    document.getElementById('ecar-topup-confirm-btn').style.display='none';
  } else {
    document.getElementById('ecar-topup-confirm-btn').style.display='inline-flex';
    const srcLabel=ecarTopupSource==='sr'?'stock room':'trailer';
    body.innerHTML=shortItems.map(item=>{
      const need=item.req-item.has;
      const avail=item.avail;
      const suggested=Math.min(need,avail);
      const cantFull=avail<need;
      return`<div class="topup-item${cantFull?' warn':(avail===0?' warn':'')}">
        <div class="topup-item-name">${ecar_esc(item.name)} <span style="font-family:monospace;font-size:10px;font-weight:400;color:#888">${item.sku}</span></div>
        <div class="topup-stats">
          <span>Has: <strong>${item.has}</strong></span>
          <span>Required: <strong>${item.req}</strong></span>
          <span>Needs: <strong style="color:#856404">+${need}</strong></span>
          <span>${srcLabel.charAt(0).toUpperCase()+srcLabel.slice(1)}: <strong style="${avail===0?'color:#721c24':''}">${avail}</strong></span>
        </div>
        ${cantFull?`<div class="topup-warn">⚠ ${srcLabel.charAt(0).toUpperCase()+srcLabel.slice(1)} only has ${avail} — will still be ${need-avail} short${avail===0?' (none available)':''}.</div>`:''}
        <div class="topup-transfer">
          <label>Transfer from ${srcLabel}:</label>
          <input type="number" min="0" max="${avail}" value="${suggested}" id="tt-${item.id}" ${avail===0?'disabled':''}/>
          <span style="color:#888;font-size:11px">of ${avail} available</span>
        </div>
      </div>`;
    }).join('');
  }
  document.getElementById('ecar-topup-overlay').classList.add('open');
}
function ecar_closeTopup(){
  document.getElementById('ecar-topup-overlay').classList.remove('open');
  ecarTopupCtx=null;
}
function ecar_confirmTopup(){
  if(!ecarTopupCtx)return;
  let moved=0,warnings=0;
  const ctx=ecarTopupCtx;
  const getSrc=(item)=>ecarTopupSource==='sr'?item.srQty:item.trQty;
  const setSrc=(item,qty)=>{
    if(ecarTopupSource==='sr'){ecar_syncSrAcrossCatalogs(item.sku,qty);}
    else{ecar_syncTrAcrossCatalogs(item.sku,qty);}
  };

  if(ctx.type==='car'){
    const parts=ecar_partsForGroup(ctx.gid);
    const shortItems=parts.filter(i=>i.qtys[ctx.carIdx]<i.reqQty);
    shortItems.forEach(item=>{
      const inp=document.getElementById('tt-'+item.id);
      if(!inp||inp.disabled)return;
      const transfer=Math.min(Math.max(0,parseInt(inp.value)||0),getSrc(item));
      if(transfer>0){
        item.qtys[ctx.carIdx]+=transfer;
        setSrc(item,getSrc(item)-transfer);
        moved++;
        if(item.qtys[ctx.carIdx]<item.reqQty)warnings++;
      }
    });
  } else if(ctx.type==='ws'){
    const shortItems=ecarWsParts.filter(i=>i.qtys[ctx.wi]<i.reqQty);
    shortItems.forEach(item=>{
      const inp=document.getElementById('tt-'+item.id);
      if(!inp||inp.disabled)return;
      const transfer=Math.min(Math.max(0,parseInt(inp.value)||0),getSrc(item));
      if(transfer>0){
        item.qtys[ctx.wi]+=transfer;
        setSrc(item,getSrc(item)-transfer);
        moved++;
        if(item.qtys[ctx.wi]<item.reqQty)warnings++;
      }
    });
  } else if(ctx.type==='trailer'){
    /* Restock trailer from SR */
    const trMap=new Map();
    [...ecarHmsParts,...ecarGobParts,...ecarWsParts].forEach(item=>{
      if(!trMap.has(item.sku))trMap.set(item.sku,item);
    });
    trMap.forEach((item,sku)=>{
      const inp=document.getElementById('tt-'+item.id);
      if(!inp||inp.disabled)return;
      const transfer=Math.min(Math.max(0,parseInt(inp.value)||0),item.srQty);
      if(transfer>0){
        ecar_syncTrAcrossCatalogs(sku,item.trQty+transfer);
        ecar_syncSrAcrossCatalogs(sku,item.srQty-transfer);
        moved++;
        const trMin=Math.max(2,item.srMin);
        if(item.trQty+transfer<trMin)warnings++;
      }
    });
  }
  ecar_closeTopup();
  ecar_renderAllViews();
  if(moved===0){ecar_toast('No items transferred');return;}
  if(ctx.type==='trailer'){
    if(warnings>0)ecar_toast(`Trailer restocked — ${warnings} item${warnings>1?'s':''} still below minimum`,4000);
    else ecar_toast('Trailer fully restocked ✓');
  } else {
    const locName=ctx.type==='car'?`Pit ${ctx.carName}`:WORKSPACES[ctx.wi].name;
    if(warnings>0)ecar_toast(`${locName} topped up — ${warnings} item${warnings>1?'s':''} still below required`,4000);
    else ecar_toast(`${locName} fully topped up ✓`);
  }
}

/* ═══════════════════════════════════
   RENDER ALL
════════════════════════════════════ */
function ecar_renderAllViews(){
  if(ecarActivePage==='cars')ecar_renderCars();
  else if(ecarActivePage==='workspaces')ecar_renderWorkspaces();
  else if(ecarActivePage==='trailer')ecar_renderTrailer();
  else if(ecarActivePage==='stockroom')ecar_renderStockRoom();
  else if(ecarActivePage==='master')ecar_renderMaster();
}

/* ═══════════════════════════════════
   CSV / DRIVE
════════════════════════════════════ */
function ecar_getCSV(){
  const h=['Type','Name','Bin #','Category','Req Qty',
    '222','226','227','223','224','225','222G','223G',
    'WS','TB1','TB2','TB3','TB4',
    'SR Qty','SR Min','Trailer Qty'];
  const rows=[
    ...ecarHmsParts.map(i=>['HMS',i.name,i.sku,i.cat,i.reqQty,...i.qtys,'','','','','',i.srQty,i.srMin,i.trQty]),
    ...ecarGobParts.map(i=>['GOB',i.name,i.sku,i.cat,i.reqQty,'','','','','','',i.qtys[0],i.qtys[1],'','','','','',i.srQty,i.srMin,i.trQty]),
    ...ecarWsParts.map(i=>['WS',i.name,i.sku,i.cat,i.reqQty,'','','','','','','','',i.qtys[0],i.qtys[1],i.qtys[2],i.qtys[3],i.qtys[4],i.srQty,i.srMin,i.trQty]),
  ];
  return[h,...rows].map(r=>r.map(c=>`"${c}"`).join(',')).join('\n');
}
function ecar_localCSV(){
  const a=document.createElement('a');
  a.href='data:text/csv;charset=utf-8,'+encodeURIComponent(getCSV());
  // REMOVED: a.download=document.getElementById('ecar-fname').value||'ECar_Inventory_Dashboard.csv';
  a.click();ecar_toast('CSV downloaded');
}
async function ecar_saveToDrive(){
  // REMOVED: const btn=document.getElementById('ecar-save-btn');
  const msg=document.getElementById('ecar-sync-msg');
  const fname=document.getElementById('ecar-fname').value.trim()||'ECar_Inventory_Dashboard.csv';
  btn.disabled=true;btn.textContent='Saving…';msg.textContent='';
  const updated=new Date().toLocaleString();
  try{
    const res=await fetch("https://api.anthropic.com/v1/messages",{method:"POST",headers:{"Content-Type":"application/json"},
      body:JSON.stringify({model:"claude-sonnet-4-20250514",max_tokens:1000,
        mcp_servers:[{type:"url",url:"https://gcal.mcp.claude.com/mcp",name:"gcal"},{type:"url",url:"https://gmail.mcp.claude.com/mcp",name:"gmail"}],
        messages:[{role:"user",content:`Save CSV as "${fname}" in Google Drive (replace if exists). Updated ${updated}.\n\n${getCSV()}\n\nConfirm with link.`}]})});
    const data=await res.json();
    const text=(data.content||[]).filter(b=>b.type==='text').map(b=>b.text).join('\n');
    const urlMatch=text.match(/https:\/\/drive\.google\.com\/[^\s)"<]+/);
    if(urlMatch){document.getElementById('ecar-drive-status').innerHTML=`Saved ${updated} — <a href="${urlMatch[0]}" target="_blank" style="color:#185FA5">Open ↗</a>`;msg.textContent='Saved ✓';ecar_toast('Saved to Drive ✓');}
    else if(/saved|created|uploaded|success/i.test(text)){document.getElementById('ecar-drive-status').textContent=`Saved: ${updated}`;msg.textContent='Saved ✓';ecar_toast('Saved to Drive ✓');}
    else{ecar_toast('Drive write unavailable — use ↓ CSV',4000);}
  }catch(e){ecar_toast('Error — use ↓ CSV',4000);}
  btn.disabled=false;
  btn.innerHTML='<svg width="12" height="12" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2.5"><polyline points="22 12 16 12 14 15 10 15 8 12 2 12"/><path d="M5.45 5.11L2 12v6a2 2 0 002 2h16a2 2 0 002-2v-6l-3.45-6.89A2 2 0 0016.76 4H7.24a2 2 0 00-1.79 1.11z"/></svg> Save to Drive';
}
async function ecar_loadFromDrive(){
  const msg=document.getElementById('ecar-sync-msg');
  const fname=document.getElementById('ecar-fname').value.trim()||'ECar_Inventory_Dashboard.csv';
  msg.textContent='Loading…';
  try{
    const res=await fetch("https://api.anthropic.com/v1/messages",{method:"POST",headers:{"Content-Type":"application/json"},
      body:JSON.stringify({model:"claude-sonnet-4-20250514",max_tokens:4000,
        mcp_servers:[{type:"url",url:"https://gcal.mcp.claude.com/mcp",name:"gcal"},{type:"url",url:"https://gmail.mcp.claude.com/mcp",name:"gmail"}],
        messages:[{role:"user",content:`Read file "${fname}" from Google Drive. Return ONLY raw CSV, no markdown.`}]})});
    const data=await res.json();
    const text=(data.content||[]).filter(b=>b.type==='text').map(b=>b.text).join('\n').trim();
    const lines=text.split('\n').filter(l=>l.trim());
    if(lines.length>1){
      ecar_parseAndLoad(lines);ecar_renderAllViews();
      msg.textContent='Loaded ✓';ecar_toast('Data loaded from Drive ✓');
    }else{msg.textContent='Not found';ecar_toast('"'+fname+'" not found',4000);}
  }catch(e){msg.textContent='Error';}
}
function ecar_parseAndLoad(lines){
  const newHms=[],newGob=[],newWs=[];
  let hi=100,gi=200,wi=300;
  for(let i=1;i<lines.length;i++){
    const c=lines[i].split(',').map(x=>x.replace(/^"|"$/g,'').trim());
    if(c.length<21)continue;
    const type=c[0],name=c[1],sku=c[2],cat=c[3],req=parseInt(c[4])||1;
    const sr=parseInt(c[19])||0,srm=parseInt(c[20])||1,tr=parseInt(c[21])||0;
    if(type==='HMS'){
      newHms.push({id:hi++,name,sku,cat,reqQty:req,
        qtys:[parseInt(c[5])||0,parseInt(c[6])||0,parseInt(c[7])||0,parseInt(c[8])||0,parseInt(c[9])||0,parseInt(c[10])||0],
        srQty:sr,srMin:srm,trQty:tr});
    } else if(type==='GOB'){
      newGob.push({id:gi++,name,sku,cat,reqQty:req,
        qtys:[parseInt(c[11])||0,parseInt(c[12])||0],
        srQty:sr,srMin:srm,trQty:tr});
    } else if(type==='WS'){
      newWs.push({id:wi++,name,sku,cat,reqQty:req,
        qtys:[parseInt(c[13])||0,parseInt(c[14])||0,parseInt(c[15])||0,parseInt(c[16])||0,parseInt(c[17])||0],
        srQty:sr,srMin:srm,trQty:tr});
    }
  }
  if(newHms.length)ecarHmsParts=newHms;
  if(newGob.length)ecarGobParts=newGob;
  if(newWs.length)ecarWsParts=newWs;
  ecarNextHmsId=ecarHmsParts.length+100;
  ecarNextGobId=ecarGobParts.length+200;
  ecarNextWsId=ecarWsParts.length+300;
}
